Dɛw gye dɛm akyɛdze n'.

Na W'enyi sɔ 'koma a ɔdze

CAN 136
5 . Mo nkwa ne mber nyinaa mu
M'bɔtow W'ayɛyi bio.
Na muwu so a, 'kyirkyir wiadzem'
W'adɔe na m'bɛtaa do:

CAN 136
6 . Mebɛma ayɛyindwom do ama W'
Mbersantsen mfesantsen,
Na onnyiewiei mpo yɛ tsia dɛ,
Wɔdze yi W' ayɛw wie!

CAN 137
1 M'asɛm na mo ndwom ara nye yi,
Mekamfo m'Agyenkwa adzekyee nyina.
. Siar dasedzi- dɛ Jesus yɛ medze!
Ao, Nyame enyimnyam nkahwɛ bɛn ny' i!
Nkwagye dzifo nye m', Nyame atɔdze;
No Sunsum awo m', bɔgyaa n' ahor m'.

CAN 137
2 . Ahobrɛasdze koraa, enyigye koraa,
Abɔfo fi sor sian ba bɔbɔ
Ahotsetɛ epue m'enyi do wora;
Mbɔbɔrhu na dɔ ho amandzɛɛ.

CAN 137
3 . Ahobrɛdze koraa, ne nyina adwe,
Menya Agyenkwam' ahomka nye siar;
Moroweɔn, rotweɔn, m'enyi tua sor;
N'ayamuyie amee m', mahera No dɔm'.

CAN 138
1 . Ao, bra ma yendzi dɛw,
Afei menya Nyame ho dɔ,
Ɔdɔ a ɔkyɛn sika.
Sɛ nkan n' meyɛ hianyi a,

CAN 138

Afei menya Otumfo a
N'abaw weɔn me dabaa.
Sɛ nkan n' motɔɔ bahaw a,

CAN 138

Dɛ mensan m'Egya fie.
Nyame dze No dɔ atwe me
Sɛ nkan n' mobɔɔ ekὸ a,

CAN 138
4 . Ao, bra ma yendzi dɛw,
M'Agyenkwa Jesus abɔtwe m'
N-kyɛ me kra reyew;
Wɔ bɔn na abɔnsam nsa.

CAN 138
5 . Ao, bra ma yendzi dɛw,
Afei menya Nyɛnkὸ a
No dɔ kyɛn onua mpo no dɔ,

CAN 138
6 . Ao, bra ma yendzi dɛw,
Ao, 'wo a edɔ Jesus,
Nyame N'abɔdze nyinara,
Wonsuo m' yenyi N' ayɛw.

CAN 139
1 . Ɔbra n' adandan nyina mu,
Ahokyer nye ahotɔm',
Beyi me Nyame ayɛw
M' akoma nye me gyirama

CAN 139
2 . M'botuw No nkwagye ho 'kodu
Bɔhwɛ m' enya awerɛkyekyer,
Dɛ ahokyerfo nyina
Na hɔn yaw ahera.

CAN 139
3 . O nye me nhuhor Ewuradze,
Ɔbae beyii m' fiir mu.
Ma yɛntonton Ne dzin,
Mefrɛɛ No m'ahokyer mu no,

CAN 139
4 . Nyame no dɔmtutuw twa hyia
Atseneneefo tsenabea;
Ɔma hɔn No nkwagye.
Hɔn a wɔtwer No mboa nyina

CAN 139
5 . O, bra bɔsɔ No dɔ no hwɛ,
Hɔn a wɔtwer No nokwar no,
Hɔn na wɔyɛ esiarfo.
Na woana bohu dɛ

CAN 139

Hom nyɛ No som hom enyigye,
Na hom nnkosuro hwee bio;
No so bɔhwɛ hom hia.

CAN 14
1 . Ewuradze nye mo Guanhwɛfo,
Biribiara nnkehia m';
Ɔma meda mfunoma mu,
Ogya m' kɔ nsutaae ho.

CAN 14

Na ɔma menantsew
Ne ndzeyɛtsenenee kwan no mu,
Wɔ Noara Ne dzin ntsi.

CAN 14

Na W' abaw hyɛ me dzen.

CAN 14

Wɔ m' atamfo enyim;

CAN 14

Me tsenabew daa nyina.

CAN 140
1 . M' beyi mo Bɔfo ayɛw nkwaber m',
Anaa bɛkyebo wɔ do yi.

Medze tum kɛse bɛkamfo N':
Na ber a me ndze bɛyew wum no,
Nkwa na adwen na ahom wɔ hɔ 'i,

CAN 140

CAN 140

CAN 140

Medze tum kɛse bɛkamfo N':
Na ber a me ndze bɛyew wum' no,
Nkwa na adwen na ahom wɔ hɔ 'i,

CAN 141
1 . Me kra, tsie! Ewuradze a;
Bɔnyɛnyi, ana 'dɔ M' a?
Tsie Ne ndze; ɔreka dɛ,
W'Agyenkwa na ɔrekasa n';

CAN 141

Memaa wo sum daan ekan.
Meyɛɛ wo pira edur;

CAN 141

Nyew, ɔyɛ a no werɛ befir n';

CAN 141

Ɔkrɔn kyɛn ɔsor m-po,
Ɔyɛ dzen, ɔkyɛn owu.

CAN 141

Enye M'bɛtsena M'ahenguam';
Ibohu M'enyimnyam ntsɛm;

CAN 141

Naaso modɔ, W', mosɔr Wo;
O, ma mondɔ Wo mbordo. Amen.

CAN 142
1 . Ɔtra n-hum', Wo dɔ a ho wɔ na n' a,
A ɔyɛ nyinaa.
Ɔpɛ dɛ ohu Wo dɔ no mbordo,
M'Agyenkwa Jesus; naaso me kra yi
Ne trɛ, no war, no krɔn, no bun, na ne dzen

CAN 142

M'Agyenkwa Jesus; naaso m'ano yi
Na ɔwo dɔ no, ɔka kyerɛ abɔn a
Pɛ dɛ dɔ a otum yi afɔdzi suro,
Wɔbɛn, wɔtwem'.

CAN 142

Nyankopɔn nkyɛn n'.

CAN 142
4 . Jesus Agyenkwa, fa Wo dɔ n' hyɛ m' ma!

Ma montɔ nkɔ noara ho wɔ gyedzim'
Mmfa beebi bio.
Na mma da biara pɛn onnkwetsir Wo

CAN 142

Ber n', No dɔ no mbrɛ otwa pa nyina,
Bɛyɛ mo ndwom.
Minya ahengua n' enyim kotow da bi a,
Ne trɛ, no war, no krɔn, no bun, na ne dzen

CAN 143
1 . Me Jesus, modɔ W', minyim dɛ medze nye nye W',
Me Jesus, sɛ madɔ w' da a, ɔno nye ndɛ.
Mo Pomfo domfo, m'Agyenkwa nye Woara,
Wo ntsi migyaa bɔn ho enyigye nyinara;

CAN 143

Me Jesus, sɛ madɔ w' da a, ɔno nye ndɛ.

Na epaa kyɛw maa m' wɔ Calvary dua no do;

CAN 143

CAN 143

Mobɔtontom Wo na matsena W'enyim daa;

CAN 144

Wɔ Nyame mu.

CAN 144

CAN 145
1 . Mema m'akoma do
Ana nkabɔm' dzendzen bi kyɛn iyi:

Na Wodze nye m'
'Wo nye m'adze nyina,

CAN 145

Ɔdze me atakyer Wo ho dzendzen.
Enam W'afɔrbɔ n' do
Eyɛ medze.
Na tsitsir dɛ,
Wo dɔ nkyehoma n' adwer m' dɛɛdɛw bi,

CAN 145

Minyim nyinam',

CAN 145

Medze dza ɔsom bo suma Wo dɛn,

CAN 145

'Wo na Wo nkorɔfo bɔm' kor afebɔɔ. Amen.

CAN 146
1 . Dɛ mbrɛ ɔtwe haahaw nsunwin ho

CAN 146

CAN 147
1 . Mobɔhom ha ara afebɔɔ

CAN 147

CAN 148
1 . Israel Guanhwɛfo, na medze

Na ewia ne hyew nn-ka hɔn.

CAN 148

CAN 149

CAN 149

CAN 149

CAN 149

CAN 150

CAN 151

CAN 152

CAN 153
1 . Bra, bɔsoɛ me! Mebue abow n' sesei;

CAN 154
1 . Mihia Wo Mber Nyina,

CAN 155
1 . Jesus, me Gyefo, Nua, Nyɛnko,

CAN 155

Sɛ Woara Wo Sunsum nye m' tse

CAN 155
3 . Nna ma ɔnda ho ɔnhyɛ me dzen,

Na mma onngyaa m' hɔ ara da,

CAN 155
4 . Sɛ mofom fi kwan pa nom' a,

CAN 155
5 . No ngo krɔnkrɔn a ofi sor

Nda ho nkyekye mo werɛ, nkyerɛ m' kwan,

CAN 156

Mbrɛ abɔfo yi No ayɛw,
Wonya adzekyee nwoaraba n'.

CAN 173

Akɛfa Ewuradze Christ,
Christ bɛhɛn mo mu hɔ ntsɛm,
Efi ewufom' aba?

Nye me abɛtsena daa.

Woana besian bun n' mu,

CAN 173

CAN 175

CAN 181

CAN 193

Bɔ m'akɔndɔ mbeamuduam'
Ma mundu botae n' ho;
Mutu me nan a ɔnnyɛ,
Na gye me pɛ fi me nsam'.
Na Wo nna wɔdze Wo yɛ

CAN 193
2 . Kyerɛ m'kwan, 'Hoɔdzen Farbaa,
Mbrɛ metse na dza mowɔ
'Mi, meyɛ akowaa koraa.
Nnkotum dze m'aba Wo hɔ.
'Nnyim' a meyɛ a, ɔnnyɛ da
'Wo nye Sahen, mo Wura

CAN 193
3 . Kyerɛ m' kwan, m' Egya Papa,
Ao, nkyɛ matɔ dɔnsuar koraa
Emi a me gyedzi suar.
Mennhyia Wo, Nyame Dɔfo,
Na Wo som yɛ dɛw ampa.
Sɛ mennya Wo, mennhu Wo,

CAN 193
4 . Kyerɛ m' kwan, Wiadze Kandzea,
Dɛ morobɔhom Wo nkyɛn;
Ma muntum ntutu ntaataa
Mirigya W' hɔ mayɛ dɛn?
'N-tsi migyaa moho ma W'.
Sor o, ase o, 'bi nnka W' ho

CAN 194
1 . Ewuradze, Wo dzinm' na misim',
Mikedzi me daa daa dwuma,
Wɔ dza modwen, meka, meyɛm'.
Wo nko na mesua dɛ m'bɔhwɛ W'

CAN 194
2 . Edwuma a Wo nyansaa akyerɛ n'
Ao, ma mempra mo mu nyina nyɛ,
Munhu Wo mo ndwuma nyinam',
Na menyɛ Wo pɛ a ɔsɛ n'.

CAN 194
3 . Ma memfa Wo ngyina me nyimfa,
Muntu mo ndwuma nyina nhyɛ Wo nsa.
Na mindzi dwuma a ebɛkyerɛ m',
'Wo a W'enyi tua mo mu nyina,

CAN 194
4 . Ma monsoa Wo kɔndua harhar n'
Na ber biara mohweɔn, monsɔr,
Na monhwɛ bɛkyebo ndzɛmba,
Nyɛ ntsɛm ndu W'enyimnyam da n' mu.

CAN 194
5 . Biribiara a W'adom dze akyɛ m'
Ma memfa nsom Wo enyigyem',
Memfam Wo ho nnantsew nkɔ sor.
Na memfa dɛw nsi m'empire,

CAN 195
1 . Ao, mo Wura, ma menye W' nnantsew
Boa me ma memfa dɔ kasa
Dwumadzi ne yaw, dadwen no dur;
Kyerɛ m' W'esumasɛm, boa m' ma monsɔw,
Kyerɛ me ma mingya akobɔfo,
Memfa hɔn nsi sor kwan no mu.
Mpuhim akoma nyaanyaa bi:
Som dwumadzi mbrɛadze kwan mu;

CAN 195
2 Amen.
. Kyerɛ m' W'abotar; ma menda ho
Asomdwee a Wo nko ara dze ma,
Awerɛhyɛm' a odzi bɔn do,
Dwumadzi a ɔhyɛ gyedzi dzen,
Dze hyerɛn nda a ɔreba kwan mu,
Enyidar a ɔtow nserɛmɛn
Mo Wura, ma menye Wo nnantsew mu.
Ntsena Wo fɛkuwbɔ dɛɛdɛwm',

CAN 196
1 . M'egya, minyim me bra nyina
Akyekyɛm' ama me,
Ɔper sɔ W'enyi daa.
Dza meserɛ nye adwendahɔ a
Munnsuro dɛ m'bohu;
Na nsakyer a otwar dɛ ɔba n'

CAN 196
2 . Meserɛ Wo adwendwen ɔdɔ a
Ɔnye 'koma a ɔpow noho
Ɔyɛ aweɔn ho nyansa,
Dze ma ahomkafo enyigye,
Na ɔtse ma binom so.
Pata nyinsuwakyifo;

CAN 196
3 . Monnhwehwɛ ɔpɛ ɔnnda hɔ komm,
Ɔhwehwɛ akɛsedze ɔayɛ
Mepɛ dɛ meyɛ abɔtoaba a
Na oehu esumasɛm;
Odzi akɔnaaba,
Woara gye me taataa.

CAN 196
4 . Wiadze mu mbrɛ m'bɛfa biara,
Mayɛ Mo Wura edwuma.
Menye nkorɔfo edzi nkitaho a
Meper ara ma oeenyin,
Na medze ahobrɛadze nye dɔ
No mu dzibew biara,

CAN 196
5 . Meserɛ daadaa ahoɔdzen a
Ɔdan mbrɛ mahyɛ W' enyimnyam
Ɔnye adwen a onnhwinhwin
Mepen som biara do.
Na ɔka Woara ho daa;
Yebisa a hɛn nsa ka n';

CAN 196
6 . Som biara a Wo pɛ kyerɛ me no
Ɔyɛ Wo mba adehye n';
Mennyɛ ho akɔmpew;
Na ɔdɔ etuhoakyɛ bra
Na me kra ehu nokwar n' a
Yɛ adehyedzi koraa.

CAN 197
1 . Hom a hom enyi tsim
Hɛn Wura No ayɛw;
Nkɛpem dɛ yebopue N'enyim.
Wɔmma yentu ntsen Jesus mu
Wɔmma yɛnyɛ kor nyi
Zion kwan do, hom mbra,

CAN 197
2 . Mber nyina yɛda ho
Ɔdomankoma dɔ fie no.
Kɔ sor kokwaa no ho
Kwantunyi fonafo fie;
Sor Jerusalem fofor no
Tow kɔ hɛn man no ho,

CAN 197
3 . Ma daa nyina yennya
Bɔn, wiadze, wu, na hɛllm';
Dɛ woeyi hɛn efi
Gyedzi ho asomdwee,
Hɔ yeekehyia hɛn Nua panyin n'.
Hɛn yɛbɔkɔ hɛn Egya fie,

CAN 197
4 . Hɛn Nua, Agyenkwa, Tsir
Ɔno nye hɛn nsɛfo esiarfo n';
Ɔyɛ hɛn adze nyin;
Hɔ hɛn akwantu bɔbɔ adze.
Hɛn a yɛka No do n'
Yebohu N'enyim ntsɛm,

CAN 198
1 . Bethel Nyame, 'Wo a Wo nkorɔfo
Ɔwò a igyaa tsetse mpanyin
Dan Wo na wonya dzi;
Hɔn akwantu nyinam'.

CAN 198
2 . Yɛdze nsewdzi na mpaabɔ ba
Hɔn mba so hɛn Nyame.
Hɛn egyaam Nyame, yɛserɛ Wo, yɛ
W'adom ahengua enyim;

CAN 198
3 . Ɔbra n'akwan nyinara mu
Gye hɛn anamɔn taataa;
Ma hɛn hɛn daadaa edziban
Na hɛn efuradze so.

CAN 198
4 . O trɛ W'atsaban wɔ hɛn do
Hɛn Egya fie asomdweem'.
Kɔ hɛn akwantu ewiei,
Na hɛn akra eetum edu

CAN 198
5 . Dɛm n-hyira na yɛserɛ
Fi W'adom n-samu;
Na kyɛpɛn afebɔɔ.  Amen.
Yɛdze Wo yɛ hɛn Nyankopɔn

CAN 199
1 . Israel akodɔm Sahen,
Hɛn ewiei, Ewuradze N'enyimnyam.
Hɛn tum, W'adom; hɛn mbra, W'asɛm;
Sor akwantufo hɔn kwangyafo,
Wo dɔ mununkum kata hɛn do;
Wo nwinwin ase na yɛtse,

CAN 199
2 . Dɛ Wo Sunsum gya hɛn yi dze,
Ber a ɔdɔ kɛse bɛn hɛn.
Mbusu nye suro bɔkɔ ekyir,
Yennhia dɛ daa wɔkyerɛ hɛn kwan,
Yɛnnkɔfom hɛn Nyame kwan no;
Yɛnnkɔfom kwan wɔ sar yi do;

CAN 2
1 . NYIMPA a hom wᴐ wiadze nyina,
Hom mbra N'enyim hom mbedzi dεw.
Hom mfa enyigye ndze ntow ndwom:
Hom mfa nyi Nyankopᴐn ayεw;

CAN 2
2 . Ewuradze yε Nyame ampa;
N’edzidzibea do nguan nye hεn.
Yεyε Nedze, ᴐnyεn hεn daa;
Ͻnoara na ᴐyεε hεn;

CAN 2
3 . O hom nhεn N'aponkεse mu;
Hom mbedzi dεw N'abanguado;
Hom nyhira N', nyi Ne dzin ayεw;
Na hεn Nyame fata ndaase:

CAN 2
4 . Osiandε Ewuradze yε pa;
Na ᴐnnkᴐbᴐ adze ara da.	Amen.
N'ehumbᴐbᴐr so tsim hᴐ daa;
No nokwardzi si pi ampa,

CAN 20
1 . Minsi dɛn mondɔ me Nyame,
Minsi dɛn nhu N' adom no war,
Minsi dɛn nyi N' ayɛw?
Ne trɛ, no krɔn, no bun?

CAN 20
2 . W' adom tsen du obiara do,
Ɔto adasamba nyina;
Ɔwɔ hɔ afebɔɔ.
Na onnyi mbanano;

CAN 20
3 . Odu wiadze tɛtɛr nyina,
Ɔtrɛ ma onngya baako mpo,
Ne trɛ nnyi mbanano;
N-kyɛ ɔpaa mo ho.

CAN 20
4 . Mo mfom nyinii dur sorsor no;
Christ no mu edoom me fakyɛ,
Fakyɛ a wɔnnto n' abaw.
W' ehumbɔbɔr traa hɔ;

CAN 20
5 . Sor abɔfo bɛn botum akyerɛ
Ao, ma monsɔ monhwɛ.
W' akyɛdze a onnyi kabea yi,
Wo nkwagye dɔ n' no bun?

CAN 20
6 . Bra ntsɛm, adom Ewuradze,
Bɛfa Woara Wodze;
W' adaworom, bɛyɛ m' akoma
W' ahengua afebɔɔ.     Amen.

CAN 200
1 . Agyedzifo hɔn Kwankyerɛfo a
Ber a yɛnam ɔbra kwan mu.
Bra na enye hɛn so mbɛtsena,
Dze hɛn sunsum adan Wo nko
lgya sor akwantufo kwan,
Yɛpɛ yɛatwer Wo nkotonoo,

CAN 200
2 . Ahɔho nye amamforafo,
Hɛn domakoma fie wɔ sor.
Na yetwa mbusu bɔnsa yim',
Wiadze ha ɔnnyɛ hɛn tsenabew;
Yɛpɛ ntsɛm yeedu hɛn kurom',
Yɛper dɛ yebohu W'enyim,

CAN 200
3 . Yennyi mantsimadze wɔ ha,
Jerusalem kurow krɔnkrɔn a ɔ
Tsease Nyame ɔkyekyeree n'.
Yɛhom do nantsew kɔ noho,
Yɛhwɛ kurow a wonnhu no kwan;
Yereper yeedu kan mbew no do,k

CAN 200
4 . Yɛdze abotar tu empire n',
Fi ahoɔdzenm' kɔ ahoɔdzenm',
Hɛn mbɔdzembɔ nyina nye dɛ,
Hwehwɛ Jerusalem fofor n';
Yegya fona wiadze 'i ekyir:
Yenya Jerusalem fofor n'.

CAN 200
5 . 'Wo a asoa hɛn bɔn nyina kɔ,
Hɛn 'nyimnyam Hen N'ahenkurow no,
Na adom hɛn bɔnfakyɛ kwa,
Yɛdze adwontow yɛsan Zion;
Yɛnam Wo do kɔ hɛn sor fie,
Yɛrotow ndwom nna ɔrebɛn hɛn.

CAN 200
6 . Nyame dɔ ne mfar ma hɛn do
Nu hɛn ahoɔdzen mu kɔ kan
Yɛakɔdɔm mbakan Asɔr no,
Yɛdze dɛw bɛyɛ abɔtsir
Yeekehyia hɛn Sahen wɔ sor.
Yɛrokɔ Nyame bepɔw n' do

CAN 201
1 . Gya hɛn, ɔsor Egya, gya hɛn
Gya hɛn, weɔn hɛn, kora hɛn, nyɛn hɛn,
Naaso yɛwɔ nhyira nyinak
Sɛ Nyame ne hɛn Egya a.
Wɔ wiadze po pramee do,
Yennyi boafo dɛ Wo nko,

CAN 201
2 . Agyenkwa, fa hɛn bɔn kyɛ hɛn;
Eyɛɛ ankonam, dze berɛ,
Hɛn mberɛwyɛ nyina Ɔwo nyim;
Na fona kyiin sar no do.
'Wo dzii hɛn kan nantseew wiadze,
'Wo tsee no mu yaw wenwen;

CAN 201
3 . Hɛn Nyame Sunsum a 'risian,
Edom, dze kyɛ, weɔn hɛn yi dze,
Fa sor dɛw hyɛ 'koma ma,
Hwere rennsɛɛ hɛn asomdwee.
Na yɛmfa ɔdɔ mbɔ dɔ mu,
Wɔ enyigye a ɔnnsɛɛ dam',

CAN 202
1 . Gya m', Kan dɔyɛfo wɔ sum a etwa ehyia yim'
Gya m' ara kɔ!
Mbrɛ kan hɔ tse, namɔn kor ara ma m'.
'Nago n' yɛ sum, menye fie ntam' so war;
Weɔn m'anamɔn, mimmbisa dɛ munhu

CAN 202
2 . Nkyɛ menntse dɛm, monnsɔɔr pɛn dɛ Woara
Gya m' ara kɔ.
Modɔɔ apɔmpɔmpɛ, na musuro mpo a,
Nkyɛ mefa mo kwan, na muhum', afei
Ntsɛn hyɛɛ me ma, mma nnkaa mfe a-etwam' kɔ.
Woara gya m' ara kɔ!

CAN 202
3 . Wo tum ehyira me dze, ɔbɛda ho
Atra sar, abo na nsu, 'kɛpem dɛ
Egya m' akɔ
M'bohu hɔn bio dɛ wɔreserew kyerɛ m'.
Na adze kye a, adɔfo a mayew hɔn n'
Sum yi bɛpa;

CAN 203
1 . Gya m', O gya m', Jehovah tumfo,
Fa Wo tum nsa n' suo mo mu;
Kwantunyi a menam sar do;
Meyɛ mberɛw, 'wo yɛ hoɔdzenfo;
Nyɛn me ndɛ na mber nyina.
Sor edziban!

CAN 203
2 . Bue nsunyiwa hyɛnhyɛnn n' sesei,
Gyefo tumfo!
Ma ogya na mununkum fadum
Mbrɛ yarsa nsu fi pem no;
Ngya m' m'akwantu nyina mu:
Yɛ mo mboa na me kyɛm daa.

CAN 203
3 . Na mudu Jordan nkɔnkɔnoa a,
Ayɛyindwom
Bɔ mo suro ham ma ɔnhera;
Fa me kodu Canaan sɔnn.
Na medze m'bɛma Wo daa.
Wu no kumfo, hɛll ne sɛɛfo,

CAN 204
1 . O adom Hen, fi sor ahengua n' do
Fa dɔ hwɛ na tsie hɛn mbɔbɔr su.

CAN 204
2 . Hwɛfo pà a edze bɔgya tɔɔ Wo nguan,
Kora Wo nguankuw a wɔnnkyɛr kwan fom.

CAN 204
3 . O Pomfo pa, Wo wu mu na agye hɛn:
Ma abɔn awerɛhofo daa nkwa.

CAN 204
4 . Sor Edziban, yɛdze Wo nyɛn hɛnho:
Pin bɔboa hɛn akra hɛn hia ber mu.

CAN 204
5 . Apatasu, ndzebɔnyɛfo Dɔfo,
Edɛw na siar nsunyiwa a ɔnnsa da.

CAN 204
6 . Ao, fa sor adom kyekye hɛn werɛ;
Yi W'enyim fɛɛfɛw n' enyimnyam kyerɛ.

CAN 204
7 . Adzekyeem' mununkum, adzesaam' ogya,
Bɛn hɛn na dan hɛn sum ma ɔnyɛ kan.

CAN 204
8 . Nye hɛn nnantsew, nye hɛn kwan daa daa,
Hɛn nkwam' na wum' Werɛkyekyer, Tum, Gyafo.

CAN 204
9 . Fa Wo dɔ enyi n' gya hɛn kwan daa daa,
Na fa hɛn du hɛn sor fi nom' sɔkyee. Amen.

CAN 205
1 . DZEBƆNYƐNYI kɔbesae a mahaw,
Ɔbra n'ehum rutu, kwanm' ayɛ kɔnn,
Ɔdomankoma, mma nnto me seraha.
Ɔkra no Kwangyafo, gya m' kodu sɔnn.

CAN 205
2 . Gya m' kodu fie, me kra no korabew,
Mbrɛ ankonam bɔbɔfo biara nnyew.
Me bra n'ewiei to m' a, Onyankopɔn,
Samanadze Kanea, gya m' kodu sɔnn.

CAN 205
3 . 'Wo a kitsa samanadze saafee
Akra a woenya Wo no wɔnnhwehwɛ hwee;
Annkɔa -wɔnnkɔ Christ e, gya m' kodu sɔnn.
'Wo yɛ Nokwar, Ɔkwan, N-kwa ma abɔn;

CAN 205
4 . Sum mu etumfo pii risi me mpa,
M'adɔntsenhen tumfo! gya m' kodu sɔnn.
Naaso ber a medan Wo Nyame dɔ n',
Woetwa ayer m'; minnya beebi memfa;

CAN 205
5 . Medan Wo gya a, mabra; adze ehu m';
Ankor-n'apem-Nyame, gya m' kodu sɔnn,
M'adagyaw mu, boa me menyɛ tartweɔn:
Motwer Wo a, mewie, owu nnkotum me;

CAN 205
6 . Sɛ 'Wo Christ gyà m' a, mowɔ asomdwee;
Dɛ ekyim o, ntsɛm o, gya m' kodu sɔnn.
Me hia mu W'asɛm yɛ m' edzi-amee;
Migyaa moho ma Wo Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,

CAN 206
1 . Ebufuw da! Ao, nyinsuwa da!
Dza nkɔnhyɛfo kae n' abam',
Sor nye asaase rotɔ nso.

CAN 206
10 . Eku Woho ara ahwehwɛ m',
Aso dɛm adom yi nyɛ gyan?
Atɔ m' wɔ fona mbeamudua n' do;

CAN 206

Ansaana werdzi da n' aso.
Dom hɛn brafi ho bɔnfakyɛ,

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

Onsiesie noho mma atsɛmbu.

CAN 206
18 Amen.
. Ao, Nyame, hu n' mbɔbɔr na gyaa n',
Dom hɛn W'ahomgye a onnyiewiei.
Tse ma hɔn a Jesus ehyira,

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 206

CAN 207
1 . Ewuradze, ɔnnyɛ 'mi m'asɛm

Muwu anaa metse ase o;
Yi gyedɛ W'adom ma.

CAN 207
2 . Sɛ nkwa war a, m' enyi bɛgye

Dɛ m'botu akɔ onnyiewieim'?

CAN 207
3 . Christ ɔmmfa m' ndua mbrɛ hɔ yɛ sum

CAN 207

CAN 207
5 . Na m'botwa mo suhuhun do,
Jehovah N'ayɛyi.
Makɔdɔm esiarfo a wɔtow
Na fona na bɔn ndafua,

CAN 207
6 . Me nyimdzee wɔ hɔ bra n' ho suar,
Gyedzi enyi yɛ kusuww;
Na ɔdɔɔ so dɛ Christ nyim Ne nyina,
Na menya N' bɛkɛtsena.

CAN 208
1 . Man bi wɔ hɔ a dɛw mapa wɔm',
Adzekyee nko, adze nnsa da,
Ahotsewfo dzim' hen;
Hɔ enyigye tu yaw.

CAN 208
2 . Hɔ na nhaban wuna dabaa.
Na hɔ nhiren nnyam da;
Sorman na hɛndze yi ntamu.
Wu tse dɛ po tseabaa a, otwa

CAN 208
3 . Nhaban huanhuam wɔ esuegya hɔ
Dɛ Jordan pem twa ntamu.
Dɛm na Jewfo hun Canaan ma n'
Woewuna dukuduku;

CAN 208
4 . Na adasa suro bɔ piriw dɛ
Wɔbɔ ngyangyan wɔ esukɔn do,
Wobotwa po tseabaa n',
Wosuro dɛ wobepia.

CAN 208
5 . Ao, nkyɛ yeeyi ekyingye akwa,
Canaan a yɛdɔ no.
Na adwen kusukusu n',
Na yɛdze enyi a do tsew eehu

CAN 208
6 . Nkyɛ yaafow mbrɛ Moses kegyinae n',
Jordan esu anaa owu nwin,
Na yaankwɛ noho mbew n',
Runntu hɛn bo wɔ hɔ.

CAN 209
1 . Jerusalem, m'ahomka fie,
Dzin a ɔsom me bo,
M'edwuma bɔbɔ adze dabɛn
Wɔ wo siar asomdweem'?

CAN 209
2 . Dabɛn na m'enyiwa bohu
N-kwagye ahyɛ w'aban dzen,
W'abrɔn mu hyerɛn sika.
W'afasu nye mbotsen?

CAN 209
3 . Ehɔ nhyiren n' kyɛn Eden turem';

Na bɔn nye yaw nnyi hɔ:
Per kɔ siar bea yi do.

CAN 209

CAN 209

CAN 21

CAN 210

CAN 210

CAN 210

CAN 211

CAN 216

CAN 220

2 . Ao, akra esiarfo na
A wɔsom wɔ hɔ daa!
Ao, esiarfo nye hɔn
Hɔn a wɔfow
Wɔsɔr bea a Nyame tsie,
Wɔtonton Wo,
Wɔyɛ esiarfo
Zion kokwaa n'!

CAN 226
3 . Wofi ahomm' kɔ ahom mu,
Dze bodu hɔ.
Dze hɛn pɛ anan
Hɛn Hen Nyame
Kɛpem dɛ obiara dzi nyim,
Kɛpem dɛ obiara pue sor,
'Nyimnyam egua!
Wɔ nyinsu bɔnsa yim',

CAN 226
4 . Nyame nye hɛn 'kokyɛm,
Ɔbɔdom hɛn
Hɛn kan na akoban;
Ne nsamu akyɛdze ma,
Nkorɔfo nyina
Nkwagye adom,
Nye enyimnyam so.
Yenya hɛn nhyira fir mu

CAN 226
5 . Nyame dɔ No nkorɔfo,
Akra krɔnkrɔn botoo n',
Ɔnnkan hɔn Ne ndzepa:
Dɔm Ewuradze
Hɔn a wɔsɔ N'enyi n'
Nyia ne kra twer
Siarfo mprɛnsa.
Wo nkotoo n', yɛ

CAN 227
1 . Wo sor abangua yɛ fɛw,
Ao, mo sunsum no kɔn dɔ
Ha so W'abangua yɛ fɛw,
W'amayɛ n', Adom Nyame!
W'asɔrmba hɔn fɛkuwbɔ,
Wɔ bɔn na mbusu man yim'
Wɔ kan na dɔ man no mu;
W'enyim ne hyerɛn fɛɛfɛw n',

CAN 227
2 . Abɔso Nyame, nnoma a
Hɔ na hɔn enyi gye daa.
Na akra a wɔhom sor Egya
No bom' no, woewie dodow!
Oennya 'saase do sibea n',
Wɔsan kɔ hɔn hɛn no mu,
Wɔtse dɛ ebubur n' a
Wosu kyin Wo fie, woewie!

CAN 227
3 . Woewie ampa! hɔn ayɛyi
Dze kodu W'ahengua n' ho;
Edziban fi sor nyɛn hɔn.
N-su pue sar do ma hɔn,
Pem mbusu bɔnsa 'i mu mpo;
W'anan ho na wobom som,
'Wo a agye hɔn ne nyinam'.
Wofi ahom mu kɔ ahom mu,

CAN 227
4 . Mo Wura, ma muntu ehu dɛm:
Adom nye enyimnyam fir Wo;
Fa W'adom no suo mo mu,
Gya m' twa bɔn wiadze yi mu;
Gya mo mfom 'koma 'i, weɔn no;
Ma minnya kwan wɔ Wo nkyɛn.
M'ewia nye me kyɛm nye 'Wo;
O mo Wura, hue gu mo do.   Amen.

CAN 228
1 . M'akoma dzii ehurusi
Afahyɛ da nye ndɛ.
Bra ma yɛnkɔ Nyame Ne fie;
Dɛ me mfɛfo see dɛ,

CAN 228
2 . Hɛn anan bɛyɛ ntsɛm
Ahɛn asɔrdan nom'
Ber a mobra na mpanyin pii
Rehyɛ som-bea no ma.

CAN 228
3 . Ebusua wɔtɔ dɛ
Ehumbɔbɔr egua n'enyim
Wɔbɔ punkum ba ha;
Wɔdze dɛw kotow hɔ.

CAN 228
4 . Sɔr ma Jerusalem,
Nyame ntɔ Ne nhyira ngu hɔn a
Nyankopɔm ahenkurow n';
Wɔdɔ Ne fie papa.

CAN 228
5 . Ha 'i dze wɔmma koryɛ
Na asomdwee ntsintsim daa;
W'ahemfi amaama.
Zion, ahonya pii nhyehyɛ

CAN 228
6 . Hɛn afɛ nye enuanom
Nnkɛpa hɛn mpaayim' da;
Nyame mma N'asomdwee!  Amen.
Wohyiam' asɔryɛm' ara pem a

CAN 229
1 . Jesus, fa wusoɛr tum n'
Ɔnyɛ mber krɔnkrɔn.
Gyina hɛn finimfin;
Ma hɛn asɔryɛ yi

CAN 229
2 . Hue Wo Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn
Akra nyina mu.
Gu akoma nyina do;
Tu suro na yaw fi

CAN 229
3 . Na yebemia mu dzen
Bɛkyebo da n' kwan.   Amen.
Dɛ hɛn enyiwa da
Yeetu hɛn kwan yi,

CAN 23
1 . Jesus dzin bɔ adze nyina do,
Abɔfo na nyimpa kotow n',
Na mbɔnsam fi enyim guan.
Wɔ hɛll, nye ase, nye sor,

CAN 23
2 . Jesus! dzin a ɔyɛ abɔn dɛw,
Ɔhotse hɔn suro nyina,
Dzin a wɔdze akyɛ abɔn;
Na ɔdan hɔn hɛll yɛ heaven.

CAN 23
3 . Jesus! otu adaduafo apo,
Ɔdze tum hyɛ nyia onnyi ahom,
Na ɔma ewufo nkwa.
Otsia abɔnsam tsir do;

CAN 23
4 . Ao, nkyɛ N' adom ahonya no
Adasamba nyina.
N-kyɛ No dɔ abaw n' bofua
Wiadze nyina aasɔ ahwɛ!

CAN 23
5 . Ne tsenenee na No nkwagye
M' edwuma nye dɛ mekam' dɛ,
Na mobɔ no dawur,
Wɔnhwɛ Eguambaa no!

CAN 23
6 . Edɛw bɛn na nkyɛ ɔbɛyɛ,
Dɛ mo wumpa no do,
Dɛ, Wɔnhwɛ Eguambaa n'!
Mobɔbɔ Ne dzin na matseam'

CAN 230
1 . 'EWimbir ansaana wi rotɔ n'
Ao, dɛw bɛn nna wɔammfa annkɔ!
Ao, yaw horow bɛn nna ɔannka hɔn!
Ewuradze, nna ayarfo gu W' nkyɛn;

CAN 230
2 . Bio, edu 'wimbir, na hɛn so
Sɛ Yennhu wo mpo a, ɔyɛ dɛn?
Yɛdze yarba horow twe pin;
Yenyim na yɛtse dɛ 'wɔ ha.

CAN 230
3 . Agyenkwa Christ, pam hɛn mbusu,
Binom so ayew dɔ a wonyae.
Na binom abɔm,
Na binom nndɔɔ W' nokwar mu pɛn,

CAN 230
4 . Binom hu dɛ wiadze yɛ gyan,
Binom hɔn mfɛfo how hɔn werɛ,
Naaso wɔmmfaa Ɔwo nnyɛɛ nyɛnko.
Naaso wonntum mmfi wiadze nsa;

CAN 230
5 . Ewuradze hɔn nyina serɛ ahomgye,
Hɔn a wɔper asom Wo yie n'
Na wobefi bɔn mu koraa;
Nna wohu bɔn a ɔwɔ hɔn mu.

CAN 230
6 . Agyenkwa Christ, Nyimpa nye W' so;
Ema Wo dɔ enyi do a, ihu
Epirakur a fɛr dze rusuma n'.
Wɔatseetsee Wo, wɔasɔ W' ahwɛ;

CAN 230
7 . Wo nsaano wɔ tum dɛ tsetse n',
Ewimbir bɔw nwinwin yim' tsie,
Na W'ehumbɔbɔbɔrm' sa hɛn yar.
W'anomusɛm biara nnkefir gyan;

CAN 231
1 . Nyame, fa Wo nhyira gya hɛn kwan,
Ao, hyɛ hɛn dzen
Dom hɛn dɛw na asomdwee;
Ma ankorankor yennya Wo dɔ
Mfa ndzi nkwagye adom ho dɛw;
Wɔ bra sar akwantu yim'.

CAN 231
2 . Yɛdze ndaase na ntonton ma W'
Asow hɛn akoma nye bram';
Nkyɛ Wo nkwangye no ho aba
Nkyɛ Woara so
Wɔ Wo nsɛmpa dɛɛdɛw n' ho;
Yeehu W' hɛn nkyɛn afebɔɔ.    Amen.

CAN 232
1 . Asɔr ne fapem kortoo
Ɔdze No bɔgyaa tɔɔ no
Ɔnam nsu nye N'asɛm do
No nkwa ntsi na owui.
Nye Jesus Christ hɛn Wura;
Ofi sor bɔhwehɛɛ no.
Yɛɛ n' N'abɔdze fofor.
Yɛɛ n' N'ayefor krɔnkrɔn.

CAN 232
2 . Wɔpaam' yii n' aman nyinam',
Adom nyina wɔ mu.
Dzin krɔnkrɔn kor na ohyira;
Enyidar kor na ɔper ho,
Naaso ɔyɛ Asɔr kor.
N'edziban krɔnkrɔn kor,
No nkwagye tum ɔnye yi-
Wura kor, gyedzi kor,

CAN 232
3 . Sɛ mpo nyimpa si atwetwe
Ahotsewfo n' weɔn, wosu
Anago su n' nnkyɛkyɛr na
Ɔadan anapa ndwom.
Dɛ mpaapaam' atsetsew mu
Dɛ, ondu da bɛn ara?
Hwɛ N'ahokyer kɛse,
Nkyerɛkyerɛ bɔn tseetsee N' a,

CAN 232
4 . Berɛ nye amandzehu mu,
Bɛhɛn n' ahomgye mu.
Ɔmmbɔ adze n' n'emudzi n',
Ɔtweɔn daadaa asomdwee a
Kɛpem dɛ n'enyi bohu
Na Asɔr konyimdzifo no
N'akodzi dede n' mu,
'Nyimnyam enyidado n',

CAN 232
5 . Na ɔwɔ wiadze yi, ɔnye
Ɔkorsa Nyame bɔm',
Dɛ abrɛfo yinom, ma
Dzi nkitaho dɛɛdɛw.
Ewuradze, dom hɛn,
Na ɔnye hɔn a wɔrohom
O ahotsewfo esiarfo!
Yɛnye W' mbɛtsena sor hɔ.  Amen.

CAN 233
1 . Nyame kurow mbrɛ odua so
Na n' afasu war a!
'Nokwafo nye W' adehye dɔm,
Wɔ mbew na mber nyinam'.

CAN 233
2 . Asɔr krɔnkrɔn kor, nkodɔm kor,
Botae a ɔkrɔn kor,
Ɔhen Otumfo kor.
Dwumadzi kuw kor, ndɔbaa ndwom kor,

CAN 233
3 . Ofitsi nyimpa n' ahyɛse
Mbrɛ W' aman esi atserɛw
Mbrɛ W' asɛm esi edwir n'!
Wɔ ahotɔ na dɔm' a!

CAN 233
4 . Mbrɛ Wo gya si dzɛw anago
Dze kɛpem adzekyee.
Dze weɔn na ɔnnhwer a!
W' akoban hyerɛn sunm' ara

CAN 233
5 . Asorɛkye bu akɛse kwa,
Anhwea dwurudwuruw gyan;
Bɛkyebo kurow si do n'.
Onntum mmpuhim botantsim a

CAN 234
1 . Wɔka wo ho enyimnyam nsɛm,
Ebɛn botum awosow w'?
Ebɛserew w' atamfo.
N-kwagye yɛ wo ho afasu;
Nyia ɔnnsan N' asɛm no kyekyeer
Tsetse Bo no nye wo fapem,
Wo dɛ No kurow a ɔtsenam'.
Zion, hɛn Nyame Ne man;

CAN 234
2 . Hwɛ, n-kwa nsu a ofi Nyame
Adom a ɔpem daa nyina
Hia ho suro fi hɔn do.
Ma wo mba wɔmee, na oyi
Ne daadaa dɔ mu pem no
Wɔ dɛm esutsen yi ho?
Wo Nyame dze dom wo daa.
Woana na ɔbɔtɔ bitsi

CAN 234
3 . M' Agyenkwa, menam W' adom do
Ɔno mpo bɛyɛ mo ntuw,
Enyigye nye ahonya a otsim
Ma wiadze nsi me atwetwe,
Mofora Zion mamfom' a,
Nye ahokyerɛ resen.
Wiadze nye no mu enyigye
Zion mba nko na wonya

CAN 235
1 . Yɛda ho yɛtse nkwam'?
Christ N' adom a ɔapon hɛn ntsi
Hom mma yenyi N' ayɛw.
Yeehu hɛn enyim bio?

CAN 235
2 . Nyame tum akora hɛn
Wɔ nkwagye a odzi mum';
Yɛbɔm' bio wɔ Christ N' ayɛyim',
Yedzi N' enyim ehyia.

CAN 235
3 . Mbusu pii a yeehu a!
Akodzi a yeeduam' a!
Fitsi dɛ yehyiaa nkan n'.
Guado ɔko', na hɛn mu hu' a!,

CAN 235
4 . Ewuradze No dɔ
Agye hɛn ne nyinam',
Na ɔda ho dze No mboa ma hɛn
Na osie hɛn nkwa wɔ sor.

CAN 235
5 . Dɛm a hom mma yentuw
Kɛpem dɛ yeetua bɔn.
No nkwagye tum no mu,
Tum a ɔgye hɛn nkwa koraa

CAN 235
6 . Hom mma yɛmfa mbeamudua n'
Dza aka n'- yemmbu no hwee
Na yeenya ahenkyɛw n';
Sɛ yebenya Jesus Noara a

CAN 236
1 . Ma hɛn honam ndzi mpaa
Hɔn akoma yɛ kor.
Jesus N'adɔfo dze, dabaa
Nkɔ mbew horow do mpo;

CAN 236
2 . Jesus na odzii kan
Ɔma yɛka koryɛm'.
Dze hɛn akoma bɔɔm';
Hɛn a yɛnye N' nantsew fufuwn'

CAN 236
3 . O wɔmma yɛnkɔ do
Asɔr ne Tsir konyimdzifo n',
Wɔ Jesus N'edwumam';
Yɛnka No do ndzi nyim.

CAN 236
4 . Christ no wenyin ture n'
Da sor hɔ rotweɔn hɛn.
Na hwɛ! akatua kɛse no
Saw n'edwumafo enyim;

CAN 236
5 . O hɛn 'koma nye adwen
Mbrɛ hɛn fona bɔ adze.
N-da ho ara mfow sor,
Nkɔhwɛ hɛn ahomgye bea no,

CAN 236
6 . Hɔ dwumadzen nyina,
Hɔ yehyia a yɛmmpaam' bio.
Nye amandzehu nye yaw
Wotwa do wɔ siar mpoano hɔ;

CAN 236
7 . Ahomka bea dɛɛdɛw,
Hɔ na abɔfo hyia hɛn,
Hɔ yebohu hɛn enyim bio,
Na yeekyiakyia hɛnho.

CAN 236
8 . Abakamfo Asɔr,
Hɔn nhyira n' yebenya,
Na yɛdze dɛw ayɛ abɔtsir
Yɛakɔ sor ahomgyem'.

CAN 237
1 . Christ a nhyira nyina fir Wo,
Ema ahosewfo dzi mu,
Tsie hɛn a Wo su sɛ hɛn,
Yɛyɛ Wo honam nwanwa n'.

CAN 237
2 . Ka hɛn ho wɔ sunsum korm',
Ɔwo a ehyɛ adze nyina ma.
Ma yɛnda ho nya Wodze n';
Yɛba bebisa mbordo,

CAN 237
3 . Kenyan, nunu na gya hɛn
Kyɛn ankorankor akyɛdze,
Ma hɛn ndwuma nyina nhyɛ ma.
Wɔahyehyɛ n' dɛ mbrɛ epɛ,

CAN 237
4 . Dɛw mu ara yɛnyɛ kor
Na yɛmboa hɛnho nkorkor;
Obiara nyɛ n'afamudze.
Yennya tsema mma hɛnto:

CAN 237
5 . Ɔdɔ tse dɛ wu, ɔasɛɛ
Christ yɛ adze nyinam' adze nyina.
Edzin, ekuw nyina gu
Mpaapaamu na adehyesɛm nyina

CAN 238
1 . Jesus, 'nye W' Asɔr ntsena,
Wɔrosɔ ne gyedzi ahwɛ n',
Yɛ n' Agyenkwa, Wura, Gyafo;
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
2 . Tsew ne bra na nkyerɛkyerɛ ho;
Dom n' abotar ma ɔnsɔw
Na ɔntwer W' anohoba n',
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
3 . Ma ne ndze nyɛ wansa daa;
Ɔmbɔ nkaa wɔ atsɛmbu ho;
Ɔnka Agyenkwa pa ho nsɛm,
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
4 . Tsetsew ne nkyehoma mu;
Dom no ɔsor asomdwee n',
Tseam ma ko na 'nyiber ngyaa;
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
5 . Ongya ehiafo na efurafo,
Ɔnkyekyer 'koma bobɔe,
Nda ho nhwehwɛ dza ayew n',
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
6 . No nokwar kanea n' nhyerɛn;
Ɔmma ne kan n' do wɔ sor
Wɔ abosom-man sum mu.
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.

CAN 238
7 . Ma ne nyimdzi nyɛ krɔnkrɔn;
Ɔmboa aman nyina ngu;
Ɔnka bɔn no dɔm nyina ngu;
Yɛserɛ Wo, tsie hɛn.    Amen.

CAN 239
1 . Guanhwɛfo pa, dom hɛn Wo mboa
Fa ma Wo mba nyina.
Tum a wɔdze weɔn, wɔdze sɔr,
Wɔ hɛn mbusu nda yim',

CAN 239
2 . Ber a yɛda ho da nsɔhwɛm',
Ber a yɛso mbeamudua 'i,
Ma yɛmfa hɛn kra nto Wo do
Wɔ mpaabɔ a ɔmmbɔ adzem'.

CAN 239
3 . Ma yendua gyedzim' hɛn nsa nka
M-paabɔ sunsum no;
W' enyim nye Wo dzin pa n'.
Yemmia ndzi ako gyedɛ yehu

CAN 239
4 . Ma 'koma biara nsu nka dɛ:
Gyedɛ ama m' dɔ a odzi mu,
Minnkegyaa Wo ma akɔ,
Na edze Woho akyɛ m'.

CAN 239
5 . Minnkegyaa Wo ma akɔ gyedɛ
Ebɔ Wo dzin kyerɛ m',
Ma meyɛ dɛ Ɔwo.
Na egye me kra nkwa nwionn nwionn,

CAN 239
6 . Ekyir no ma munhu W' enyim
Mbrɛ wɔmen gyedzi nye mpaabɔ
Wɔ adzehu nye ayɛyim'.  Amen.
Wɔ kokwaa n' etsifi,

CAN 24
1 . Eguambaa bi, nkwagye dzin bi,
Dɛ Wo nkotoo.
Enyidar bi nnyi sor anaa ase,
Fɔdzi nye fɛr ho guansumabew bi nnyi,

CAN 24
2 . Me gyedzi suar, m' enyidar suar,
Kekam' frɛ Wo.
M' akoma ne hia nye no mbusu nko
Na ɔbɔ mu dɛ senaman wɔ mo mu

CAN 24
3 . Kaansa muwu a, Ɔwo yɛ nkwa;
Gyedɛ Woara.
Meyɛ nwim mpo a, mo Wura, dɔ ne gya nye W'
Minnyi etsidaa, minnyi fie biara so

CAN 240
1 Ber a yɛkotow Wo yi,
Bra behyira hɛn sesei.
Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Sian, ao Ewuradze domfo, sian!
. Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Bɔ Wo ndze a onyan ewufom',
Ewuradze, kyerɛ Wo tum;
Na ma Wo nkorɔfo ntse.

CAN 240
2 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Ma akra nhwehwɛ nkwa-su n':
N-kwa edziban no!
O ma hɛn esunsum kɔn ndɔ

CAN 240
3 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Krɔn W' enyimnyam dzin no;
Mma W' nye Wo mba nyina.
Wo sunsum mma hɛn dɔ m-fram

CAN 240
4 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Ma W' asɛm no nnya tum;
Ma wɔmfa enyikan gyedzi ntsie
W' asɛmpa a nhyira wɔm' n'.

CAN 240
5 . Kenyan W' edwuma yi,
Na enyimnyam no bɛyɛ Wodze,
Na nhyira n' aka hɛn.
Tɔ Pentecost bɔw no;

CAN 241
1 Ahomka da! ahomka da!
Ɔkyerɛɛ m' dɛ monweɔn na monsɔr
Da a Jesus hoor mo ho bɔn nyina
Da a Jesus hoor mo ho bɔn nyina!
Na mindzi dɛw aber nyina
. Ahomka da ɔnye da n' a
Ɔsɛ dɛ mo 'koma dzi dɛw
Medze moho maa m' Agyenkwa!
Na ɔka ne dɛw kyerɛ aman.

CAN 241
2 . Siar n-hyehyɛɛ! ɔsɔw nsew a
Ber a meba N' asɔrfim' yi,
Midzii kyerɛɛ mo Dɔfo n' ano!
Wɔmma ayɛyindwom nhyɛ hɔ ma.

CAN 241
3 . Ahyɛmu kɛse no yeewie dzi!
Ɔtwetwee m' ma mekaa No do,
Mo Wura dze nye m', No so yɛ medze;
Ne Nyame ndze n' ɔyɛ me dɛw.

CAN 241
4 . M' akoma a ekyima akyɛr
Afa N' a, afa siar nyina.
Bɔhom wɔ ahomka bea ha:
Mma mmfi w' Ewuradze nkyɛn da

CAN 241
5 .  Sor man nyina a hom tsee me nsew n,
Akɛpem da a owu bɛba a
M' behyira me kra wɔ nsew yi ho.
M' besi do daa ma hom aatse,

CAN 242
1 . Hwɛ mbrɛ Israel Guanhwɛfo
Ɔreyɛ hɔn etuu.
Esi dze dɔ gyina hɔ;
Tsie! ɔrefrɛ m- bɔtoaba,

CAN 242
2 . Ɔse, Hom ngyaa hɔn ma wɔmbra,
Mma hom mmbu hɔn 'nyimtsia!
Na Ewuradze bae.
Osian akra yinom n-tsi

CAN 242
3 . O, Ewuradze, ndaasem' ara
Hɛn mba so nyɛ Wodze.   Amen.
Na yɛdze hɔn brɛ Wo,
Yedzi dɛw dɛ yɛyɛ Wodze,

CAN 243
1 . Ɔkofo, soɛr gyina,
Apow wiadze ndzɛmba
Fa wo Pomfo dzin ka ntam dɛ
Suo Christ mbeamudua n' mu;

CAN 243
2 . Soɛr ma wonnuma wo-
Ndɛ to wo gyedzi dzin.
'Nye wo Nyankopɔn ndzi ahyɛmu,
Wɔnhor wo ho bɔn nyina;

CAN 243
3 . Ndɛ Christ akowaa nye wo
Na asomafo n' na atɔfo n'.
Ndɛ edɔm tsetse nkɔnhyɛfo n',
Wɔkan wo fora esiarfo n',

CAN 243
4 . Ma Nyame akodze nyina
Ɔsa n' bɛyɛ dzen, ɔbɛkyɛr,
Na otwar dɛ yedzi nyim.
Nhyɛ w' dzen; 'nye abɔnsam nko:

CAN 243
5 . Konyim abɔtsir n' a!
Hɔn gyedzi bedzi nyim!
Sor ndwom dɛɛdɛw bi n' a!
Yi na Sahen n' dze ma hɔn a

CAN 244
1 . Honam a wobuu mbɔbɔrhu mu',
Bɔgya a wokyii mbɔbɔrhu mu';
Ɔwo ewu ma hɛn bɔn ewu;
Ɔwo na ekaa nkwa asɛm no,

CAN 244
2 . Hwɛ akoma a yaw epira no,
Dɛ W'adom nyɛn hɛn akra ampa.
Hwɛ nyinsu a ndzenbɔnyɛfo kyi,
Ma, W'edziban nyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze

CAN 245
1 . Ewuradze Krɔnkrɔn, memmfata
Dɛ 'Wo 'bɛba mo hɔ,
Kasa ara: ka adomsɛm kor,
Na me kra ho bɛsan.

CAN 245
2 . Memmfata: me kra mu tsenabew
Ebɛyɛ dɛn ahɛn mu hɔ?
Kasa, na m'bɛtse apɔw.
Yɛ nwinwin, yɛ nkɔnkɔw;

CAN 245
3 . Memmfata dze; na m'bɛyɛ dɛn
Ɔwo a Wo honam nye bɔgyaa
Edze tɔɔ nkwa maa me.
Mesiw me Nyame kwan?

CAN 245
4 . Obra! Anapa (Ewimbir) bɔw yi mu
Bɛyhɛ m'akoma ma. Amen.
Fa Wo dɔ nye Wo tum nyina
Fa Woho bɛnyɛn me;

CAN 246
1 . Afei hɛn Egya yɛrekaa Wo dɔ n',
Afɔrbɔdze a no nko fata W'enyim,
Dɔ a ɔtɔɔ hɛn prɛko wɔ mbeamudua n' do n';
Jesus, nokwar afɔrbɔdze a otsim.
Na hɛn sor Dzimafo n' so wɔ ha yi,
Yɛtrɛ hɛn afɔrbɔdze mu ma Wo,

CAN 246
2 . Jesus a wɔasera No n' na hwɛ N'enyim,
Ehwɛ hɛn a, hwɛ hɛn wɔ Christ no mu;
Mma nnhwɛ hɛn dɛ yeetsiatsia W'adom do;
Mma nnhwɛ hɛn mpaabɔ nye gyedzi nwinwin n':
Na hwɛ! hɛn mfom nye hɔn ho akatua,
Wo Ba, hɛn Wura, N'amandzehu so ntam'.

CAN 246
3 . Hɔn so a yɛdɔ hɔn kyɛn adze nyina n',
Bɔ mbɔdzen nyina hɔn kra ne yie ho;
Fa dzenhyɛ wie dwuma n' ma wɔnkɔ kan.
O fa W'ehumbɔbɔr fua hɔn Wo bom',
Sie hɔn krɔnn fi emumuyɛ nkekaa ho,
Yedua Christ do yɛtotɔ serɛ ma hɔn;

CAN 246
4 . N-tsi yɛaba; twe hɛn pin W'anan ho,
Agyenkwa pa a yɛafom mpo a edɔ hɛn;
Dua do yi hɛn fi mbusu nyina ho:
Edziban dɛɛdɛw mu yɛ hu yi,
Ma hɛn dɛw na fahodzi Wo som mu,
Na mma nngya hɛn mma yemmfi Wo
nkyɛn da.   Amen.

CAN 247
1 . Agyenkwa no dɔ ho nkaa ntsi
Ha na Jesus to nsa dze frɛ
Hɔn a woenu hɔnho.
Na yɛaba pon yi ho:

CAN 247
2 . Yɛnam gyedzim' fa nkwa paano
Ogui maa abɔn no.
Yɛdze nyɛn hɛn akra;
Yɛnom wenyin dze kaa bɔgya a

CAN 247
3 . Ha na yɛtow ndwom yɛkamfo
Da bi sor aponto edziban
Jesus N'anwanwa dɔ;
Na yɛsɔ hwɛ wɔ ha.

CAN 248
1 . Dɛ mbrɛ W'adom Asɛm no tse,
Ahobrɛadzem' ara
'Ruwu, mebɛkaa Wo.
Yi na m'bɛyɛ, m'Ewuradze a

CAN 248
2 . Wo honam a 'mi ntsi wobui n'
Bɛyɛ mo sor paanoo;
Ma medze makaa Wo.
W'ahyɛmudze kuraba n' na megye,

CAN 248
3 . Sɛ medan m'enyi hwɛ mbeamudua n'
Na mohom Calvary hɔ a
Nyame Egumba e, m'afɔrdze e,
Otwar dɛ mekaa Wo.

CAN 248
4 . M'bɛkaa W' ɔnnye Wo fona nyina,
M'bɛda ho ara makaa W'.
Nye Wo dɔ a adɔ m' nyina
Nyew ber a ahom kakra wɔ hɔ 'i

CAN 248
5 . Na aber a mobɔtɔ mmum
Ber a 'nam W'ahendzim' bɛba n'
Jesus, ɔyɛ a kaa me.
Na adwen na nkaa bɛhera n'

CAN 249
1 . Ma yenhu W' ber a yeridzidzi,
Agyenkwa, nye hɛn ntsena, na to
Na mma nn-dan hɛn nngya;
Wo pon hɛn 'koma mu.

CAN 249
2 . Enye hɛn ndzidzi Nyame dɔm';
N-kwa paanoo, sor wenyin no,
Nyɛ hɛn edziban daa.   Amen.
Wo honam na bɔgyaa,

CAN 25
1 . Mbrɛ Jesus ne dzin dua yɛ dɛw
Na otu no suro nyina.
Otu ne ya, yɛ ne yar edur,
Wɔ gyedzinyi asom' a!

CAN 25
2 . Ɔbɔ sunsum a oepira esu,
Ahomgye ma fonafo.
Edziban ma sunsum a kɔm dze n',
Na ɔdwe akoma a ɔahaw,

CAN 25
3 . Dzin pa! Botan a motow do,
Adom na ɔahyɛ n' ma!
M' egyapadze a ɔmmpa da,
Me kyɛm na mo sumabew,

CAN 25
4 . Jesus, mo Guanhwɛfo, mo Nua
Bra bɛgye m' ayɛyi.
Mo Sɔfoe na me Hen,
Mo Wura , mo Nkwa, mo Kwan, m' Ewiei,

CAN 25
5 . Mo mbɔdzembɔ ɔyɛ mberɛw,
M' akoma yɛ wɔɔwɔw;
M' beyi W' ayɛw dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɛ.
Na ber a m' bohu W' dɛ mbrɛ Ɔwo tse n',

CAN 25
6 . Kɛpem da n' na m' bɛka Wo dɔ no
Ɔnhom me kra wɔ wum'.     Amen.

Na ma Wo nsanku dzin dɛɛdɛw n'

CAN 250
1 . Sor paano a enyɛn me,
Ɔwo a iwui na etse ase,
Ma nokwar nkwa paano yi
Minnya Wo mu ahoɔdzen daa.
Nyɛn me kra daa daa nyina;
'Wo 'yɛ edziban ampa:

CAN 250
2 . Sor Wenyin, fa Wo bɔgyaa
Ɔwo a eyɛ mo nkwa,
Hyɛ afɔr kuraba yi ma:
Ma mintsim wo mu pintsinn. Amen.
Mohwɛ W'asɛndua n' nya nkwa;
W'epirakur ma n-kwa ,

CAN 251
1 . O Ewuradze, ha na muhu W'enyim,
Ha na mepɛ mesuo dza wonnhu mu;
Morohwehwɛ menya Nyame N'adom,
Na medze me berɛ mato Wo do.

CAN 251
2 . Ha na m'bedzi Onyame edziban,
Na makaa Wo fakyɛ ne dɛw no bio.
Na medze m'adzesoa mato n-kyɛn
Na menye Wo anom ɔsor wenyin;

CAN 251
3 . Edzidzi na adwontow aber nye yi,
Ɔsor pon na wɔato ama me yi.
Ma menye Wo mbɔ mu yendzidzi ha,
Na enye me ndzi nkitaho dɛɛdɛw.

CAN 251
4 . Ɔnnkyɛr na wɔakata nsɛnkyerɛdze n' do:
Aponto n' etwam'; dɔ no dze nntwam' da.
'Wo, hɛn Kyɛm na Ewia, ebɛn hɛn daa.
Woyi paano na wenyin no kɔ mpo a

CAN 251
5 . Minnyi mboa bi dɛ Wo nko Wodze no,
M'Ewuradze, Woara dɔɔ so ma me,
Na onnhia mpo dɛ motwer obi so.
Wo tum n-ko ara nye m'ahoɔdzen.

CAN 251
6 . Mber pii na yɛaba W'edzidziase:
Na yɛsɔ ne dɛw hwɛ ase ha yi.
Ne nyina kyerɛ hɛn sor dze kɛse no,
Sor edziban a da bi yebedzi

CAN 252
1 . Christ abɔ werdam apon hɛn,
Da a ɔbɛba.
No ho nkaabɔdze na yɛyɛ yi;
Yɛkyerɛ hɛn Wura No wu kɛpem

CAN 252
2 . No honam a wobui maa hɛn
Ɔno na ɔnyɛn hɛn dɔ kɛpem
Da a ɔbɛba.
Wɔ nkaabɔ paano yi mu ha,

CAN 252
3 . Bɔgya a oruwu a okyii no
Da a ɔbɛba.
Wenyin yi yɛ ho sɛnkyerɛdze.
Yɛbɔnom ara akɛpem

CAN 252
4 . Anago bɔn a wonyii N' mae n'
Da a ɔbɛba.
Na Ne mbae a odzi ekyir no
Yɛdze dɔ nyɛbea bɔm' kɛpem

CAN 252
5 . O, asɛm pa a ɔhyɛ hɛn dzeen!
Ɔma hɛn akomatɔmu.
Da a ɔbɛba.
Hom mma yengyina dzen nkɛpem

CAN 253
1 . N-dze a wɔtsee wɔ Eden
Asɔpɔn awar nhyira n'
Ayerhyia kan n-dze n',
Ɔda ho ara wɔ hɔ.

CAN 253
2 . Christian ɔbaa na barimba
Na yɛserɛ Ne nhyira:
Nyame Ɔkorsa wɔm' bi,
So rokɔ awar a,

CAN 253
3 . Dɛ ɔndom hɔn m-ba pa,
Biribiara nntum mmpa mu.
Na ɔndom hɔn koryɛ bi a
Nye dɔ na nokwardzi,

CAN 253
4 . Sor Egya, Woara bɛfa,
Ayefor yi ma awar,
Dɛ mbrɛ 'dze Eve maa Adam,
Fii noara ne mfem' no.

CAN 253
5 . Agyenkwa domfo, bra na
Bɔɔm' wɔ Woara Wo mu n'
Bɛka hɔn bɔm' ɔdɔm',
Dɛ mbrɛ edze su ebien

CAN 253
6 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, behyira hɔn,
Ber a wɔrobɔ mpaa yi,
Dɛ mbrɛ ehyira Christ N'Asɔr
Ma ɔyɛ N'Ayefor n'.

CAN 253
7 . Tserɛw W'atsaban wɔ hɔn do,
Ba W'afɔrmbukyia ho,
Ber a worutu anamɔn
Pa hɔn mbusu nyina,-

CAN 253

Abɔbɔ Wo afɔr,-
Kɛpem dɛ wɔnye Agyenkwa
N' Ayefor no bɔsoɛr.

CAN 254
1 . Egya, adze nyina Yɛfo,
Ɔdɔ a nokwardzi wɔm'.
Dzii kan dze akra ebien bɔɔm'
Ma Wo mbofra yi so,
N-dɛ fa nkan n' akyɛdze n'
Ofi a W'asomdwee wɔ mu,
Wɔ Eden ture mu;
Wo nyansaa, tum na dɔ

CAN 254
2 . Gyefo a ekɔr Galilee
Ayeforase hɔ,
Ɔndan sor enyingye
Dɛ Woara W'akyɛdze a.
Hɔn a wɔfrɛ Wo yi:
Ma hɔn wiadze enyigye
Na wɔsɔ hwɛ a, ma wonhu
N-dɛ so fa enyimpa ma

CAN 254
3 . O Nyame Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn,
Ama Woara wowaw hɔn
Ɔwo a Wo dɔ yɛ dzen,
Ehyɛ hɔn 'koma do.
Fi ntokwaa ho n-tsi,
Fi sor gu hɔn do ahom,
Hɔn bra aakyerɛ dɛ 'Wo na
W'ahotsewee so dzi mu,

CAN 254

Awar a ehyira do;
Ɔdɔ a Wo Sunsum tsew ho
Gyefo, Woara ennhyira do a,
Hɔn dɛw bɛdan hɔn yaw;
Na hweeara nnkotum asɛɛ
Wɔnnkɛfa edu beebi;
Yɛ dɔ a ɔmmbɔ adze da.

CAN 256

CAN 257
1 . Ewuradze, kasa kyerɛ me,
Ahwehwɛ me yi ma mo so
Ma munsusu Wo do nkasa;
Monhwehwɛ Wo mba a wɔayew no.

CAN 257
2 . Mo Wura, gya me kwan ma mo so
Manna mma hɔn a kɔm dze hɔn.
Mingya W'akobɔfo taataa;
O nyɛn me ma mo so memfa

CAN 257
3 . O hyɛ me dzen ama ber a
Maatsen me nsa ama hɔn a
Migyina pintsinn wɔ Wo mu n',
Woridzi aper wɔ bra po do.

CAN 257
4 . Kyerɛkyerɛ m' na meetum makyerɛ
Akoma pii ase noho.
Ma m'anosɛm n-hwira ndu
N-dzɛmba pa a ada n' edzi;

CAN 257
5 . Fa W'asomdwee dɛɛdɛw n' ma me,
Asomdwee nsɛm nkyerɛ Wo mba
Asonafo wɔ mbusu mber mu.
Ma minnya nyansa memfa nka

CAN 257
6 . Mo Wura, fa Wo mayɛ no ma m',
Kodu dɛ m'akoma bu do,
Ma memfa ndam mombɔ dawur,
Menka Wo dɔ, minyi W' ayɛw.

CAN 257
7 Amen.
. Fa me yɛ dɛ Woara 'pɛ,
Aber nyina na bea biara,
Kodu dɛ mubohu W'enyim
Wɔ ahomgye, dɛw, na enyimnyam ma.

CAN 258
1 . EWURADZE, hyerɛn hɛn do,
Ɔwo, adasamba Kan;
Dua Wo kyerɛwsɛm do
Eesua W'adom nwanwa n'.
Hɛn akoma dzɛw ntsi
Na yɛhwɛ W'enyim a
Nkɔkowaba nam hɛn do
Yi Woho kyerɛ hɛn ndɛ;

CAN 258
2 . Ewuradze, hue Sunsum
Gyaframee n' gu hɛn do,
Ma hɔn adwen ontsim,
Ma Wo mba aso pa,
Ma yɛdze ano kor
Na hɔn nyina eehu
Ndzɛmba akɛse a ayɛ.
Yaabɔ Wo dzin dawur.

CAN 258
3 . Hɛn Wura, kasa ma hɛn,
Ama nguambaa aatse
Dza yɛka nyina mu,
Hɔn Guanhwɛfo n' Ne ndze,
Ma dza yɛkyerɛ nyɛ dɛ
Mbrɛ W'asɛm tse ara;
Na wɔaaka No do daa,
Na woeedzi No mu dɛw.

CAN 258
4 . Hɛn Wura, tsena hɛn mu;
Aatwe Wo mba nyina.    Amen.

Na hɛn bra aakyerɛ
Na yɛdze hɛn suban
Nyina ndɔ Wo, nsom Wo;
Wo mbofra mbrɛ etse,

CAN 259
1 . N-dɔbaa Ewuradze, tsie
Na dom hɛn dza yehia.

Wo nkowaa ehiafo hɛn su;

CAN 259

CAN 259

CAN 259

CAN 259

CAN 26
1 . Pomfo kɛse, Nyame Eguambaa,
Dɛ Wo dzin nwanwa no.

CAN 26

CAN 26

CAN 260
1 . Hɛn Wura, sɛ W'asɛm ntsi

Yedua n-kwasɛm n' a,

CAN 260

CAN 260

CAN 260

CAN 261
1 . O Twearammpon Nyame,
Bubu ɔbɔn no tum.
Ma W'ahendzi no mbra,
O Christ, ma W'abaw do

CAN 261

Bɔbɔ adze wɔ ha?

Nye dɔ wɔ mu n' wɔ hen?

CAN 261
3 . W'anohoba n' wɔ hen
Akodzi nye brafun

Dɛ mber bi rebɛba a

CAN 261

Wo tum kɛse no mu,

CAN 261
5 . Nyimpa mmbu Wo dzin bi,

CAN 261
6 . Abosonsɔr dze sum
Agye aman pii do;
O Anapa Nworaba,
Pue, na mma nntɔ ara da. 	Amen.

CAN 262
1 . Wiadze ruwu; daa nyinara
Christianfo, hom m-per ngye hɔn;
Hom nka Jesus nkyѐrɛ hɔn ntsɛntsɛm.
Mpempem mpempem na wɔsen kɔ!

CAN 262
2 . Ahodze, ahoɔdzen, nyimdzee,
Hom Gyefo ayɛ bi ama hom!

Nyew, hom n-kwa mpo hom mfa mma;

CAN 262
3 . Nyame No Sunsum, fi edzi,
Keka po mu, nunu kwaa mu.

Prapra Nyame Ne mba boà ano.

CAN 263
1 Christ N'ahenman ntsi yɛsɔw ɔfona a,
Jesus akofo atamfo n' gyina a,
No som yɛ dɛw, na owu yɛ mfaso.
Wɔnper ndzi nyim, ɔkogu yɛ mbusu;
. Wɔnkɔbɔ dawur wɔ mbea nyinara dɛ,
Asomdwee Hen n' oridzi Ne hen:
N'adzesoa yɛ har, na No som so yɛ dɛw;
Wonyi No ayɛw, ahemfo hɔn Ɔhen.

CAN 263
2 . Jesus Ɔkatakyi no dɔm adehye,
Wɔ mbea nyina dɛ wiadze Agyenkwa.
Wɔnhwɛ mbrɛ Christ Ne dzin edua atahye,
Wɔnsoɛr ngyina ma adasa nnya nkwa;

CAN 263
3 . Nokwar frankaa na orinyam wim' noho n',
Ɔda na tsenenee aba wiadze;
Hɛn Wura apa hɛn sum mu amandzehu,
Jesus apon hɛn ama fahodzi.

CAN 264
1 . WƆMFÀ Asɛmpa n' nkɔ ekyirѐkyir,
Asomdwee, isiar na nkwa.
Mbrɛ wɔnntsee Jesus Ne nka.
Na mber nyinara wɔmpaa mu
Nka dɛ, Jesus bedzi Hen.
Wɔmfa dɛw nkamfo Ne dzin.
Wɔmpaam' dɛ No mu wɔ fafir,
Wɔnka N' yie ma bahatɔfo

CAN 264
2 . Wɔmfà enyigye nsi Asɛm n' do,
Na amanaman ntonton No
Na wiadze enya nkwa ndɛ!
Nse dɛ, Jesus bedzi Hen.
Nyame Ba Jesus ebowu
Obenya sor ahendzi n';
Obiara a ɔgye No dzi no
Wɔnka n' bɔkɔɔ ara dɛ:

CAN 264
3 . Enyimnyam nkã Egya Nyame
M-fesantsen mbersantsen;
Na hɛn ndwom dabaa nyinara
Nyɛ dɛ, Jesus bedzi Hen!

Wɔ mbrɛ nyimpa biara wɔ;

CAN 265
1 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus!
Hom mma N'ahen-frankaa n' do;
Konyimm' akɔ konyimm'
Kyerɛ wɔka atamfo nyina hyɛ
Ma Christ dzi hen ampa.
Mbeamudua ho nsordaafo;
Obedzi No dɔm kan fi
Onnyi dɛ ofi nsa

CAN 265
2 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus!
Hom mfa ndam ngyina mbusu ano,
Hom nduom ɔko kɛse n' mu
Hom ntsie abɛn ne frɛ;
Hom ntutu dɔm nka dɔm.
Mbarimba, afei hom nsom no
Mfa ntsia atamfo dɔm n'
Wɔ N'enyimnyam da yim'!

CAN 265
3 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus!
Edwumayɛ mu o, mbusu mu o
Hom ngyina N'ahoɔdzen nkom'
Hom nhyɛ Christian akontar,
Honam abaw bɛpa hom;
Mma hom nntwa abrɔdɔ.
Mma hom nntwer hombo da.
Na hom nweɔn asɔryɛm',

CAN 265
4 . Hom ngyina, hom ngyina mma Jesus!
Aperdzi no rennkyɛr
Bedzi hen afebɔɔ.
Ɔnye enyimnyam Hen no
'Kyena konyimdzifo ndwom a
Ndɛ dze ɔko mu dede
Nyia obedzi konyim no
Wɔbɛma n' nkwa ahenkyɛw

CAN 266
1 Christian n-sordaafo,
Dzi hɛn envim kan.
Hom nduom akono!
Jesus Ne mbeamudua n'
. Christian n-sordaafo,
Dzi hɛn enyim kan.
Hɛn Hen Christ etu sa
Hom nduom akono!
Hom nduom n-seraban do,
Hom nhwɛ ne mfrankaa n'.
Jesus Ne mbeamudua n'
Roko tsia tamfo n',

CAN 266
2 . Yɛma Ne frankaa n' do a,
Abɔnsam dɔm gu;
Dɛm a Christ akofo,
Enuanom, hom ntow ndwom,
Hɛll fapem wosow;
Hom mma hom ndze do.
Hom nkedzi konyim!
Yɛbɔ se yi ayɛw a,

CAN 266
3 . Nyame N'asɔr tse dɛ
Dɔm a wɔyɛ dzen:
Hɔn anamɔn mu.
Hɛn botae, hɛn nkyerɛkyerɛ
Hɛn dɔ nyina kor.
Hɛn mu nnyi mpaapaamu,
Yɛnam ahotsewfo
Yɛyɛ adze kor.

CAN 266
4 . Ahengua botutu,
Ahenman etwam',
Betsim afebɔɔ;
Christ Noara na ɔkae,
Na Jesus N'asɔr dze
N'asɛm so yɛ hɔ.
Runntum ahyɛ do:
Samanadze akoban

CAN 266
5 . Mo nkorɔfo e, hom mbɔdɔm
Bɔtow afebɔɔ.
Egyigye kuw yi;
Enyimnyam na nkamfo
Hɛn konyim ndwom yim':
Hom mfa hom ndze mbɔto
N-ka hɛn Hen Christ!
Yi nyimpa na abɔfo

CAN 267
1 . Ma m' gyedzi ntsaban na muntu
Mbrɛ hɔn 'nyimnyam hyerɛn pa.
Nkɔ fua n' mu hɔ nkɔhwɛ
Sor esiarfo hɔn dɛw kɛse n',

CAN 267
2 . Ber bi nna wogyam wɔ ase ha,
Dzii aper dzen dɛ hɛn so.
Na wɔkaa m' kyii nyinsu;
Wɔnye bɔn, ekyingye na suro

CAN 267
3 . M'bisa dɛ hɔn konyim n' fir hen?
Hɔn konyim fir No wu.
Hɔn konyimdzi fir Eguambaa n',
Hɔn nyina bɔ mu ka dɛ

CAN 267
4 . Wɔhyɛɛ mbrɛ otsiatsiae no nsew;
Na wɔkaa Nyame- nyimpa N' do
No ndwuma hyɛɛ hɔn nkuran,
Nyaa anohoba ahomgye n'.

CAN 267
5 . Hɛn kandzifo hia hɛn nkamfo
Kyerɛ dɛm sor kwan n' ara
Na adasefo mununkum no
Wɔ Ne fasusu ntsi;

CAN 268
1 Alleluia!
. Ahotsewfo a apon hɔn edwuma a
O Jesus, nhyira nka Wo dzin daa daa.
Wiadze enyim wɔbɔɔ Wo dzin no ntsi,

CAN 268
2 Alleluia!
. Hɔn Bontan, Aban, Ahoɔdzen, nye 'Wo,
Eyɛɛ hɔn Sahen wɔ nkodzen no mu;
Sum kadoo no mu hɔn nokwar kan kor.

CAN 268
3 Alleluia!
. O ma Wo nkowaa anokwafo wɔnko
Ama wɔnye hɔn eenya ahenkyɛw no!
M-barimbam' dɛ tsetse ahotsewfo n',

CAN 268
4 Alleluia!
. Siar nkitaho bit! fɛkuwbɔ krɔnkrɔn!
Naaso wɔnye hɛn bɔm' yɛ kor Wo mu.
Yɛper mberɛwm', wɔhyerɛn enyimnyam mu;

CAN 268
5 Alleluia!
. Sɛ aperdzi n' yɛ dzen, ko n' war m-po a,
Konyim ndwom no fi 'kyirekyir du asomu,
Ma akoko yɛ dur, abaw hyɛ dzen.

CAN 268
6 Alleluia!
. Witɔree dze sika hyerɛn wim' guann,
Ɔnnkyɛr na akofo enya ahomgye.
Wohu siar Paradise no mu dɛw no.

CAN 268
7 Alleluia!
. Hwɛ! enyimnyam da bi so ɔreba a,
Ahotsewfo n' bɔsoɛr konyimdzi mu,
Enyimnyam Hen no bopue No kwan do.

CAN 268
8 Alleluia!
. Dɔm kukuankoma fi wiadze nyina
Dze ndwom bɛpem bota mbotsen no mu,
Woeyi Egya, Ba, nye Sunsum ayɛw;

CAN 269
1 . Woanam' wɔhyɛ futuw yi,
Hɔn Wura N'asɛ ntsi wowui,.
Kan no mu mba a wodzi kan,
Wɔbɛn Nyame N'ahengua 'i?
Wɔhyerɛn sen wigyinae mpo 'i?
Wɔkaa Nyame a owu n' do n'.
Wodzii Christ ho dase pa,
Yinom na wɔsoaa mbeamudua n',

CAN 269
2 . Wofir fona kɛsem' bae,
Bɔgya a ɔma ahosan krɔnn:
Na wɔsom hɔn Wura daa daa,
N-tsi wɔbɛn ahengua n',
Nyame ko No nkorɔfo mu.
Nyame pɛ N'apapafo.
Wɔ Eguambaa n' bɔgyaa mu,
Wɔdze gyedzi hoor hɔn ntar

CAN 269
3 . Wɔkyɛn ekonyimdzifo,
Domankoma bea no do.
Ha na hɔn nsɔhwɛ asa;
Hɔn berɛ nyina etwam',
Kɔm na nsukɔm nnyi hɔ bio;
Ofir ewia ne mfirii no mu,
Wɔnntse ɔhyew a ɔyɛ dzen a
Wɔtse ahomka mbew no mu,

CAN 269
4 . Nyia ɔtse ahengua n' do n',
Bɛnyɛn hɔn aber nyina,
Bɛpa hɔn mbusu nyina,
Ɔbɛpepa hɔn nyinsuwa.
Ɔdze dɔ bɛhyɛ hɔn ma.
Dze hɔn bɔkɔ nkwa nsu n' ho;
Dze nkwadua no bɛnyɛn hɔn,
Nye hɔn ehiadze biara,

CAN 27
1 . Jesus, Wo ho adwen nko mpo
Dze dɛw hyɛ mo mu ma;
Edɛw no bɔbor do.
Na meba m' bohu W' enyim dze a,

CAN 27
2 . O adasa hɛn Agyenkwa,
Dzin biara nnto Wodze a
Na yɛadwen ho dɔ mu.
Yɛdze enyigye bɔtow ho ndwom,

CAN 27
3 . O 'koma bobɔe n' Enyidar,
Abrɛfo Enyigye,
Hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ Wo.
Iye ma asehwefo na

CAN 27
4 . Na hɔn a wohu Wo nka dɛn?
Hɔn a wɔtse Wo dɔ nko ara
Na wonyim ne dɛw no.
Wonnhu dza wɔnka mpo:

CAN 27
5 . Jesu, yɛ hɛn enyigye ndɛ,
Hɛn ndaamba akatua;
Jesu, yɛ hɛn Enyimnyam ndɛ
Na mfesantsen nyina.    Amen.

CAN 270
1 . JESUS dze nkwagye reba n'
Ɔmaa wɔkaa No do ara:
Hɔn ho annyɛ No ebufuw
Hɔn ndwom yɛɛ N' enyigye.
Mbofraba nyina soɛree
Na ɔtse abowa do n',
Wɔtoow Hosanna maa N'.
Zion hɔ na ɔbae,

CAN 270
2 . Na osiandɛ Ewuradze
Ɔhen Jesus frankaa n',
Da ho dɔ mbofra ntsi,
Kaansa n-dɛ odzi hen
Na yɛatsea n' dɛ, Hosanna
N-ka David ne Ba.
Wɔ sor Zion m-po a,
Yɛbɔfɔr Ne frankaa ho,

CAN 270
3 . Osiandɛ sɛ hɛn yeenntum
Abo bɔtow Hosanna
Ahyɛ hɛn enyito.
Dabi? Yɛdze hɛn akoma
Na aso hɛn ano nko
Na yɛdze bɔsom No?
So bɛma Ewuradze.
Yɛannkamfo hɛn Pomfo a,

CAN 271
1 Dɛ, Hosanna nka hɛn Hen.
Tsie! mbofra kekam' dzendzen
. Jerusalem mbofraba
Bɔm' tow Gyefo N'ayɛyi:
Ndɛ mber yi mbofraba so
Toow Jesus N'ayɛyindwom;

CAN 271
2 . Wɔkyerɛ hɛn Ewuradze dɔ,
Wɔkyerɛ hɛn ɔsor do kwan:
Wɔkyerɛ hɛn N'asɛm kenkan,
Yi ntsi yeyi Nyame ayɛw.

CAN 271
3 . Abaatan na akyerɛkyerɛfo,
Ma Hosanna ngyigye wim'.
Mpanyin na mbofra nhur ndwom n';
Wɔmma do kɛsenara

CAN 272
1 . JESUS brɛfo a edwe,
Hu mo botooyɛ mbɔbɔr,
Kyea W'enyi hwɛ W'abofra;
Ma me kwan membra Wo hɔ.

CAN 272
2 . Mepɛ dɛ wɔdze m' brɛ Wo;
Adom Wura, mma nnsiw kwan,
Ma W'abɔtoaba yi kwan,
Wɔ W'adom ahenman n' mu.

CAN 272
3 . Fa Wo nsa to me tsir do;
Ma menda W'abaw no mu;
Ma montwer Woara Wo bom';
Mo Wura, boaboa m' ma menda

CAN 273
1 . EWIMBER som ekyir,
Asɔrfi sunkamm no m'
Awerɛfir mu ara na
Kanea n' ayɛ munsumm,
Krɔnkrɔn 'daka n'enyim
Nyame Ne ndze ɔgyegyee hɔ.

CAN 273
2 . Nna akɔdaa brɛfo,
Ewuradze yii kyerɛ Hannah ba n'.
Israel sɔfo n' ada;
Levinyi kakraba n'
Na dza ohuntaa Eli no,
Roweɔn asɔrfi m' hɔ:

CAN 273
3 . O Ewuradze, ma me
Emi so m'bɛgye Wo frɛ do,
Na m'bedzi kan metse Ɔwo.
No mu yɛ har, ɔtse
Samuel asomkyɛn a
W'ano wasa biara;

CAN 273
4 . O ma m' Samuel akoma,
Adzekyee na adzesaa akoma a
Akoma brɛfo a ɔtweɔn
Anaa ɔweɔn W'abow;
Otsin Wo pɛ do dzi dwuma.
W'asɔrfi mbrɛ ewɔ mu

CAN 273
5 . O ma m' Samuel adwen;
Ɔyɛ setsie ma Wo,
Gyedzi pa a onnhwinhwin,
Na medze abofra enyiwa eehu
Nokwar a wɔdze esie enyansafo n'.
Wɔ nkwa na owu mu,

CAN 274
1 . Dza ɔyɛ fɛw na ɔhyerɛn,
Abɔdze nyinara,
Nyame yɛɛ ne nyina.
'Nyansadze na anwanwadze,

CAN 274
2 . N-hyiren biara a ɔpae,
Anomaba a ɔtow ndwom,
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—
Nyame maa n' ahoɔfɛw;
Nyame yɛɛ ne ntɛkyerɛ.

CAN 274
3 . Bepɔw a osi habanm',
Adzekyee na adzesaa.
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—
N-woraba na bosoom,
'Sutsen a ɔda ho,

CAN 274
4 . N-su a ɔtɔ esusow,
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—
Ewia a ɔpae pɛber,
Na hamu edziban.
N-duaba a ɔsow ndua do,

CAN 274
5 . Enyiwa wɔ hɔ ma yeehu,
Ano so ma yaaka,
Ɔayɛ adze nyina yie.
Dɛ saa Nyame yɛ tumfo,
Dza ɔyɛ fɛw—

CAN 275
1 . Modɔ dɛ metse nsɛm a
Abɔfo ndze ka no,
Bɔnyɛnyi a meyɛ mberɛw so,
Ɔbɛtsenaa asaase do.
Dɛ enyimnyam Hen n' mber bi
Dɛ, Ewuradze bae bɛgyee m' nkwa.
Na 'yi minyim petee
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m' kɛse.

CAN 275
2 . M' Agyenkwa siarfo bɛyɛɛ
Abɔdomaba dɛ emi,
Ɔnnkɔtow m' akyen ara da
Krɔnkrɔnyɛ mu akwan;
Ma ɔaakyerɛ No nkɔkowaba
Na sɛ mobɔ ho mbɔdzen
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m'kɛse.
Tsiatsia N' anamɔnm' a,

CAN 275
3 . No mbɔbɔrhu nye No dɔ n',
Ayamuyiem' dɛ monkɔ
Dɛ ɔtse m' ayɛyi.
M' bɔtow ho ndwom dɛɛdɛw;
Menkɛnye abɔfo ntow ndwom,
Muhu N' a ɔnnyɛ mpo a, minyim
Na ɔabɔ m' anohoba
Osiandɛ ɔdɔ m' kɛse.

CAN 276
1 . Ka Jesus ho n-sɛm kyerɛ m',
Ɔkwan nkyɛn ndzɛmba,
Epo do nsɛm,
Jesus No ho nsɛm,
Ka kyerɛ me.
Mepɛ metsie;
Ndzɛmba a nkyɛ mibebisa No,
Sɛ ɔwɔ ha a:

CAN 276
2 . Ma mindzi kan ntse mbrɛ mbofra
Adom ndzeyɛɛ,
Ayamuyie kasa,
Dze ɔdɔ hyerɛɛn
Jesus N' enyim.
Kɔbɔɔ N' aprɔw;
Na emi so me nsa bɛka
Ne nhyira n' bi.

CAN 276
3 . Kyerɛ m' enyinyandze a osii
Dɛ mbrɛ wɔyɛ
Jesus No ho nsɛm n',
Ka kyerɛ me.
M' Agyenkwa no:
Na mbeamudua n' a wɔdze kum
Ne yaw na Ne dɛw,
Ture no mu n';

CAN 277
1 . David ahenkurowm' prɛko bi,
Ɔbaatan dedaa ne ba bi
Jesus Christ ɔnye ne Ba n'.
Mary nye ɔbaatan pa n',
Nantwibuw tantan bi mu,
Wɔ mbowa dzidzidaka mu.

CAN 277
2 . Nyame, adze nyina Wura,
Ɔnye abɔbɔfo tsenaa ase.
Fi sor siaan asaase do;
Hɛn Agyenkwa Krɔnkrɔnnyi
M-bowadan ɔnye No dɔbea,
Ne dabew nye mpɔnkɔbuw,

CAN 277
3 . No mbofraber nwanwa nyina
Ɔdaa n' abaw mu foo n' yie.
Ɔdɔe, ɔweɔn ne na brɛfo a
Christian mbofra nyɛ setsie,
Ɔyɛɛ enyidzi na setsie;
Wɔndwe, nyɛ pa dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛe.

CAN 277
4 . Mbofra hɛn fasusu nye No,
Kakrabaa, m-berɛmberɛw;
Na hɛn dɛw onyam' kyɛpɛn.
Ntsi hɛn yaw ɔtse ma hɛn,
Onyinii dɛ hɛnara,
Osui, serewee dɛ hɛnara;

CAN 277
5 . Ɔnam No nkwagye dɔ no do
Da bi hɛn enyi bohu N'
Kɔ mbrɛ Ɔnoara oedu n'.
Na ogya No mbofra kwan
Nye Ewuradze a ɔwɔ sor;
Osiandɛ abofra fɛɛfɛw n'

CAN 278
1 . Akɔkowaba Jesus ennya adasoe;
Nna Jesus ada komm wɔ efuw no do.
N-woraba fi sorsor hyerɛɛn mbrɛ ɔda no,
Wɔdedaa N' wɔ mbowa edzidzidaka mu.

CAN 278
2 . Anantwi no sui na Ɔba no nyanee,
Naaso, hwɛ, oennsu, na mbom ɔdaa hɔ komm.
O Jesus, modɔ Wo; fi sor hwɛ mo do,
Tsena me nkyɛn araa kodu adzekyee.

CAN 278
3 . Ewuradze Jesus, meserɛ Wo dɛ
Bɛn me nkyɛn na dɔ me aber nyinara,
Hyira mbofra nyina wɔ W' abaatan dɔ mu,
Na tsew hɛn ho ama yaafata Wo nkyɛn.

CAN 279
1 Ahomka bɛka m';
Mbofra tse dɛ emi.
Oegum' arà refrɛ
Sɛ meba Jesus hɔ a,
. Sɛ meba Jesus hɔ a,
Ɔbɛkyekye m' werɛ.
Mo hom bɔtɔ mo ho;
Sɛ mo werɛ how a

CAN 279
2 . Sɛ meba Jesus hɔ a,
Ɔbɔdɔ m' ampaara,
Obetsie m' asɔr,
Owui maa mo bɔn.

CAN 279
3 . Sɛ meba Jesus hɔ a,
Akɔ man papam'.
Obogum' ara egya me
Obosuo me nsam',

CAN 279
4 . Hɔ menye mbofra pa
Bɛhyɛ ntar fitaa;
Mubohu m' Agyenkwà ampa
Wɔ sor man n' mu daa.

CAN 28
1 . Jesus, 'koma dɔyɛfo hɔn Dɛw,
Adasa Kan, nkwa Nsunyiwa,
Wiadze mu ndzepa nntum mmee hɛn,
Yɛdze kɔm yɛdan ba Wo hɔ.

CAN 28
2 . Wo nokwar si pi, ɔnnsakyer;
Iye ma nyia ɔhwehwɛ Wo,
Nyia ɔfrɛ Wo n' egye no nkwa;
Nyia ohu Wo n' N' adze nyina.

CAN 28
3 . Yɛsɔ Wo hwɛ, n-kwa Edziban,
Na hɛn kɔn dɔ yeedzi bi daa;
Na hɛn kra pɛ ma wɔaahyɛ n' ma.
Yɛnom Wo, n-kwa Esutsen,

CAN 28
4 . Hɛn sunsum haahaa hwehwɛ Wo,
Eyaa W' ano hɛn enyi gye,
Mbrɛ ɔbra dze hɛn si biara,
Yesuo Wom' a siar aka hɛn.

CAN 28
5 . O Jesus, nye hɛn ntsena daa,
Ma hɛn mber pa na asomdwee;
Ma Wo kan no nhyerɛn wiadze.    Amen.
Yi bɔn no sum nyina wɔ hɔ,

CAN 280
1 . Mepɛ mesũa Jesus:
Ɔyέ ayamuyie;
Obowui agye m' nkwa,
Wɔbɔɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

CAN 280
2 . Sɛ mokɔ Jesus hɔ a,
Ɔbɛma mo hὸ atsew,
Ɔdze m' bɔn bɛkyɛ m'.
Obetsie m' asɔr,

CAN 280
3 . Mobɔdwen Jesus ho:
Ɔhwɛ m' ase ha.
Ɔtse N' ahenguam hɔ,
Ɔyɛ dɔ dodow

CAN 280
4 . Sɛ mo werɛ twer Jesus,
Biribiara nnkɛyɛ m'.
Nna m' ahom bɛka m' ho,
Sɛ meyɛ Ne pέ a,

CAN 280
5 . Yamùyiefo pa Jesus!
Ɔman papa n' mu.
Na ewiei n' ɔaagye m' ato
Nkyɛ oeesuo me nsam',

CAN 281
1 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Ber a adze akye bio,
Wɔ adzekyeem' adom ho.
Yebu ntwɛr wɔ fie hyira Wo,

CAN 281
2 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Ber a yeetu hɛn ndwom wɔ skuul,
Dabaa yɛdze W' ayɛyi hyɛ
Dwumadzi ase, yɛdze wie.

CAN 281
3 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Abɔfo tsie, wɔweɔn hɛn,
Christ no nguambaa anago nyina.
Wɔ hɛn ndwomm' ana yɛada;

CAN 281
4 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Nnyɛ ayɛyi nsɛm mu nko;
Nokwardzi na setsie mu so
Yɛkyerɛ Woara W' enyimnyam.

CAN 281
5 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Dɛ ɔnam Jesus ara ntsi
Na yeku ɔbɔn biara.
Yɛdze abotar sɔw mfom nyina,

CAN 281
6 . Daa daa nyina yɛtonton Wo,
Gyedɛ hɛn nda bɔ adze,
Gyedɛ yɛhom fi hɛn berɛm',
Yɛrotweɔn Wo da n' asomdweem'.

CAN 282
1 . Ewuradze, fa Wo nhyira dom hɛn,
Bɔ hɛn ho ban
Dɛ ebɛn hɛn daa nyina.
Ma yentu anamɔn nkɔ kan
Wɔ Wo dɔ, gyedzi na surom';
Yebehyia mu bio wɔ ha;

CAN 282
2 . W' ehumbɔbɔr ho yɛsɔr Wo,
Edze dom hɛn kwan nyinam',
Ma hɛn edwuma nkɔ do daa
Ma hɛn sunsum
Na adwen nnya W' akyɛdze pa.
Nyame yetwa hwe W' enyim bio

CAN 282
3 Mpaamudzi
. Ma fidua mu enuadɔ ntsim
Akoma biara mu daa,
Bohu dɛ hɔn Egya nye W'.
Ndu dɛ Wo mba
No tum nkyerɛkyerɛ hɛn ma
Yenyi pɛsɛankonya akwa

CAN 282
4 . Nyame fa Wo nhyira gya hɛn kwan,
Fa nnuhofo nyina mfom kyɛ hɔn;
Mmfom Wo Sunsum ara bio.
Na mma Wo mba
Wonnya mber mfa ntsen dza asɛɛ n'
Yɛda ase na ehumbɔbɔr;

CAN 282
5 . Ma Wo Sunsum pa no nkenyan
Fa Wo tum kɛse n' siw ano,
Na dza ndzebɔn dze na nyina nsɛɛ,
Na yɛmper daa
Ndzepa biara a yeenya n' ha,
Nnya nyimdzee na dɔ mapa.

CAN 282
6 . Egya baatan, kora hɔn a
Bafuu ofi ber to ber;
Ehyiadzi
Hɔn a wɔresan n'
Ma dza woedua n' nsow aba pa
Nnyɛ anokwafo nsen nkan' n'.  Amen.

CAN 30
234 Saase pa do

. Jesus, hɛn Guanhwɛfo,
Ne ndze yɛ hɛn dɛw;
Ɔwasa kakra ara a
Nna hɛn enyim mpo a,
Ne ndze n' odo wɔm';
Yɛmmpɛ kwankyerɛfo biara
Dɛ No nkotoo.

. Jesus, hɛn Guanhwɛfo,
No nguan ntsi owui;
No bɔgyaa enuma
No nguambaa nyina.
Ɔwo dza odze hyɛ
Hɔn mu biara nsew,
Hɔn a woyɛ Nedze no
Wɔ no Sunsum.

. Jesus, hɛn Guanhwɛfo,
N'abaw weɔn hɛn daa;
Ngyata kyin hɛn ho mpo a,
Hɔn nsa nnkaka hɛn.
Owu bɔnsa mu hɔ,
Sum huhu hyɛ mpo a,
Yennsuro mbusu biara
Yɛka wu hyɛ.

1 . Wondzi dɛw mma onua a oewu yi,
Ɔakɛtsena dɔ Eden no mu.
No wu yi yɛ no mfaso kɛse,
Oefi nsa kɔ kan man no mu,
Wɔmma yɛmfa ndwom nka no do,
Woeyi ne kra wɔ efiadze,
Woeyi no honam mpokyerɛ n' mu;
Yɛnye no sunsum mfow ɔsor,

CAN 319
2 . Hɛn nua edu ahɛndwirii hɔ,
Beebi mbrɛ asomdwee nko wɔ,
Ɔadan n' afrɛ egya ekyir.
Ɔatsew ehum nye aahow no mu,
Hɔn wɔda ho da fona pom',
Na bɔn nye yaw nn-yi hɔ bio.
Reper edu siar mpoano hɔ,
Tsiabaa yi ne nsa aka n' ahomgye,

CAN 319
3 . Hɔ na ahɛn dɔm nyina hyia,
Ɔbra n' akwantu n' abɔ adze;
Ɔnnkɔbɔ adze dabiara pɛn.
Hɔn a wɔnye Agyenkwa nantseew ha n',
Honam n' ahohia no etwam';
M-ber a wodzi n' wɔ sor no,
Na wodzi fona nye wu do nyim:
Wɔbɔ se wokyiakyia hɔnho,

CAN 32
1 . Tsie! abɔfo ruhua dɛ
Aman nyina, hom mfa dɛw
Asaase wɔ asomdwee,
Hom nye hɔn mbɔm mpaa mu dɛ,
Nyame na abɔn abɔm'.
Nye sor abɔfo ntseatseam'
Tsie! abɔfo ruhua dɛ
Wɔawo Christ wɔ Bethlehem.
Wɔawo hɛn Hen nyimnyamfo n',

CAN 32
2 . Christ a sorsor tonton No,
Ɔbaabun wotoam' ɔba!
Ɔdomankoma Ewuradze n',
Ɔpɛ dɛ ɔnye nyimpa tsena,
Hwɛ N', ɔkyɛree mpo a ɔaba.
Hwɛ, Nyame hyɛ nyimpadua!
Jesus, hɛn Immanuel.
Nyame a wɔayɛ N' onyimpa!

CAN 32
3 . Mbo, sor Asomdwee Henba!
Bae ma nyimpa eennwu bio,
Ɔdze N' enyimnyam too nkyɛn,
'Dze kan na nkwa brɛ wiadze,
Ma ɔaama asaasemba do,
Ma ɔaama hɔn awo-enu.
Mbo, Ndzeyɛts' enenee Ewia!
Yarsa wɔ N' atsaban mu.

CAN 320
1 . Ber a dwumadzi da asa n',

CAN 320

W' adom asɛm no nhyɛ ma-

CAN 320

Kan ara afebɔɔ.

Ma yenhuahua dɛw kan no-

CAN 320
4 . Ber a yaw atsɛ akoma
Dɛw ara afebɔɔ.
Fa hɛn kɔ mbrɛ nyinsu nnyi n',
Ma afei oegyaa tow no,

CAN 320
5 . Ber a yɛrodwen nda a yɛasɛɛ n' ho,
Dɔ ara afebɔɔ.
Nda a ɔrennsan mmba bio n',
Wo dɔm' kyerɛkyerɛ ma yensua

CAN 320

CAN 321

CAN 323

CAN 324

CAN 325

CAN 325

CAN 326

CAN 327

CAN 34
1 . O Christianfo, hom nnyan na adze akye,
Anapa yi na wɔwoo Agyenkwa;

Hom nsoɛr na hom ntonton Nyame dɔ,
Mbrɛ Nyame bɛbrae ma ɔbaabun woo N'.

CAN 34
2 . N-guanhwɛfo a wɔroweɔn hɔn nguan no

N-dɛ Nyame apon N' anohoba,

CAN 34

CAN 35

CAN 36

CAN 37
