Wɔdze ndwom yii Nyame ayɛw

CAN 37
6 . Enyimnyam nka Nyame wɔ sor,
Asomdwee nka 'saase;
Nyame enyisɔ nhyɛ ase
Wɔ adasa mu ndɛ.   Amen.

CAN 38
1 . Ɔsor dɔ no ɔkrɔn dodow,
Bɛtseew hɛn sum wiadze enyi.
Ɔdze Agyenkwa fi sor bae,
Ɔmaa da pa n' hyerɛɛn hɛn do,
Na tsenenee ewia no puei,
Nyame Baatan N' ayamuhyehye;

CAN 38
2 . Nyame daa edzi wɔ Christ mu,
Akɔ daa ahomgye man no '.
Dze hɛn nan esi kwan pa mu;
Dze Ne kan abɛpam hɛn sum,
Etu hɛn bɔn na enyifura,
Na hɛn akra a woenya fakyɛ,

CAN 38
3 . Ewuradze, fa Wo kan bra,
Gya hɔn twa no sunsuma mu.
Gya hɛn kɔ W' asomdwee kwan mu;
Gyedzi a otu hɛn suro no a;
Hɛn akra a wosuro wu dzen,
Ma Wo dɔ nkitsa hɛn 'koma,

CAN 38
4 . Ma W' adom ne nhyehyɛɛ nda edzi,
Gya me twa owu sum no mu
Kodu W' ahengua enyim hɔ.
Mo sunsum nyɛ Wo fie krɔnkrɔn,
Nyame a ɔbɛyɛɛ nyimpa maa m';
Yɛ me kan na mo nkwagye mu;

CAN 39
1 . Adom nwanwa, wɔawo N'
ampa!
Ɔasoa wiadze nkukunkakar.
Ɔhen Jesus, Siar Enyidar,
Nyame Akyewa ɔabra nyimpa!

CAN 39
2 . Nwanwa bɛn na metse n' wim'
Asomdwee wɔ asaase do,
Enyimnyam wo sor ma Nyame,
Enyisɔ wɔ adasa mu.
yi?

CAN 39
3 . Ao o! hom ntsie ahobowsɛm,
Ɔsor-asaase Twerammpon,
Nwanwa esi wo Bethlehem:
Wɔayɛ N' ɔbɔn ama abɔn.

CAN 39
4 . Abɔso Hen esian nyimpam',
dzidzidakam',
Mbersantsen do a otra nhum,
N'adae nye mbowa
Oeku Tamfo, ɔasɛɛ no tum.

CAN 39
5 . Yɔkaa Wo mbae, Nyame Ba
Akra nyina bɔ se kamfo:
Christ;
Enyimnyam nka Gyefo siarfo.
'Wo na abɔpon Paradise.

CAN 4
1 . DOMANKOMA ! Wo sor tsebea
Ɔtra wimuwimu n'ekyir noho.
Mbrɛ nworaba wɔkɔ aprɔw.
Yɛ fɛw dɛ mbrɛ osɛ Nyame:

CAN 4
2 . Bɔfopanyin rotow W'Ndwom a.
Ahotsewfo a woetwa ehyia.
Bom famu wɔ hɔ nyina som Wo.
N'enyim suma n'atsaban mu;

CAN 4
3 . Nyame, dɛtse na nso nyɛ dɛn?
Hɛn so yɛbɔsom hen Bɔfo:
Kɛse, Kronkronyi, Abɔso.
Yefi bɔn na huntuma m'frɛ Wo

CAN 4
4 . Wɔatse Wo nka wɔ ekyirkyir,
Ma hen adwen nyina tɔ sin.
Mbɔtoaba esua Wo dzin bɔ;
Na Wo nyansaa N'enyimnyam no

CAN 4
5 . Nyame wo sɔr, nyimpa wɔ ase,
Hɛn ayɛyi ka hɛn anomu.
Hɛn ndwom nyɛ tsia, na hɛn nsɛm nsuar,
Wo ho enyidzi sianka hɛn ndwom,

CAN 40
1 . Igyaa W' ahengua
Amma Wo wiadze ha ne mbae:
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ber a 'baa wiadze wɔ me ntsi n';
Bethlehem fie hɔ,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.
Na W' ahenkyɛw so,
Na woennya kwan wɔ

CAN 40
2 . Sor nyina gyigyee
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Bɔɔ W' adehye dzin no dawur n';
Ber a abɔfo toow ndwom
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.
Ebaa asaase do ha:
Na mbrɛadzem' ara
Na, Ɔsor Wura,

CAN 40
3 . N-sɔ wɔ etu,
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.
Dɛtse, wɔ Galilee sar do;
Na nnoma berɛbuw,
Na Wo mpa nye dɛtse,
O Nyankopɔn Ba,
Wɔ nkyindur no nwin ase;

CAN 40
4 . Ao, Ewuradze,
Ao, bra m' akomam', Ewuradze,
Ɔkwan wɔ m' akomam' ma Wo.
Dza nkyɛ ɔbɛma fahodzi;
'Dze nkasɛm no bae,
Na nsoɛ katraka
Na wɔdze atwetwesi
Wosunsum Wo kɔr Calvary:

CAN 40
5 . Sor bɔwosow bio
Ber a 'bɛba konyimdzi mu n';
Ber a 'bɛba na ebɛfrɛ me n'.
Dɛ, Kwan da ho wɔ hɔ,
Kwan da ho wɔ me nkyɛn ma Wo!
Ma Wo ndze mfrɛ me fie
Na abɔfo atow ndwom,
Na, mo Wura, m' akoma bedzi dɛw

CAN 41
1 Ewuradze a! O anwanwasɛm!
Ewuradze a, Enyimnyam Hen n' a.
O wɔnhyɛ No abɔso Hen.
Yetwa hwe N' ananadze;
. Woana na n-guanhwɛfo
Kotow No mbowadan mu hɔ n'?

CAN 41
2 . Woana na oridzi edwin
Wɔ dan kakraba mu hɔ n'?

CAN 41
3 . Woana na ɔrekyen kɔm,
Ɔreper wɔ sar do hɔ n'?

CAN 41
4 .	Woana na orusu wɔ
Lazarus ne nda do hɔ n'?

CAN 41
5 . Woana na ɔrobɔ mpaa
Esuom wɔ Gethsamane n'?

CAN 41
6 . Woana na ɔserɛ nhyira
Ma abɔn wɔ Calvary do n'?

CAN 41
7 . Woana na oefi ewufom'
Roboa hɛn, regye hɛn nkwa n'?

CAN 41
8 . Woana na No nko dzi Hen
Sor na asaase nyina do n'?

CAN 42
1 . Na nyimpa a wɔayɛ petsee yi,
Ebɛn nye adzekyee ehyia yi?
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.
Okuw n' sii ndze adze buaa dɛ,
Wɔnam ɔhyew do yi, ase ɛ?
Wentwiwenti 'i ase nye dɛn?

CAN 42
2 . Jesus nye woana? Ɔyɛ dɛn
Awɔse ndze no buaa bio dɛ,
Ɔdze bɛn twe nyimpa pii yi?
Ɔkwantsennyi a ɔresen,
Na ɔbɔ kurow ebutuw dɛm?
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

CAN 42
3 . Jesus! 'No na ɔbaa wiadze
Boduaa mbusu kwan yi mu bi n';
Etsitsifo ɔnye mpakye:
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.
'Nyifurafo dze dɛw tsiee ntseamu n':
Wɔdze ayarfo nyina brɛɛ No,

CAN 42
4 . Ɔreba bio, fi ha kɔ ha,
Ana hɛn so yɛnnkɛpaam' dɛ,
Ɔahɛn dɛ ɔrobɔsoɛ hɔ;
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.
Oegyina hɛn abobowano,
Yɛtse N' anamɔn wɔ mbeambea,

CAN 42
5 . Ao o! akobɔfo, hom mbra;
Amandzehufo dɔbea nye 'i-
Fakyɛ nye ahomgye wɔ ha;
Hom a hom efi Egya fie,
Hom nsan mbra bio mbɛgye N' adom;
Narazeth Jesus na ɔresen n'.

CAN 43
1 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se:
Bɔto Mara Mo bom'!
Bra Mo hɔ na bɔhom;
Ɔwo a aberɛ fa wo tsir,
Maberɛ, Mo werɛ ahow;
Minyaa ahomgye wɔ No mu,
Mokɔree dɛ mbrɛ metse ara,
Na ɔmaa m' enyigye.

CAN 43
2 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se:
Bɔ wo mu adze nom bi!
Ɔwo a sukɔm dze wo,
Hwɛ, mema n-kwa nsu no kwa,
Mebaa Jesus hɔ mobɔnoom
Mo nsukɔm gyaae, me kra nyaa nkwa,
Na afei metse No mu.
N-kwa esutsen n' bi;

CAN 43
3 . Metsee dɛ Jesus ne ndze se:
Ɔyɛɛ ewia maa me!
Emi nye wiadze Kan:
Hwɛ Me na adze bɛkye wo,
M' akwantu nda nyina.
Mohwɛɛ Jesus na minyaa N' ma
N-kwa Kan yim' na m' bɛnantsew
Wo kwan mu bɛyɛ kann!

CAN 44
1 . Ɔwo a wɔpemee betsiee Wo,
Ma abɔn kwan ma yɛmbɛn Wo,
Na gye hɛn adom mu ara.
Wotsiee Wo nsɛm, wɔtsee Wo tum;

CAN 44
2 . Ɔwoara na aka dɛ,
Emi meyar, mihia Wo mboa,
Mihia Wo tum a ɔgye nkwa n'.
Primprimfo nnhia oduyɛfo;

CAN 44
3 . Wo tum, nokwar na nyamedɔ,
Otu yarba dzendzen biara.
Tsim hɔ mbersantsen mfesantsen;
W' asɛm, W' adom asɛm kor mpo,

CAN 44
4 . Kaansa makyɛr esu yi bo,
Ɔbɔbɔ  m' esu ntsɛmara.
Ma mo sunsum nntum nnka noho a,
W' ano kasa bɛma masoɛr,

CAN 44
5 . Ma dɔnhwer yi nyɛ ɔgyeber;
Ao bra, me kra no Duyɛfo!
Da W' ahosan tum no edzi,
Ma munhu Wo nkwagye n' sesei.     Amen.

CAN 45
1 . Jesus frɛ hɛn! Sɛ hɛn bra po
Ɔse: Christian, ka Mo do.
Ne ndze dɛɛdɛw n' gyigye daa daa,
Wor mpo a, yɛtse Ne ndze,

CAN 45
2 . Tsetseber do asomafo n'
Kɛkaa' No a wɔdɔ No n' do.
Tsee wɔ Galilee po do n',
Wogyaa ebusua, fie nye edwuma,

CAN 45
3 . Jesus frɛ hɛn mma yɛnnsom
Ɔhwɛ ndzɛmba a wɔsom hɛn bo a,
Ɔse: Christian, dɔ M' kyɛn hɔn.
Wiadze mu ndzɛmba huhuw;

CAN 45
4 . Enyigye nye awerɛhow mu,
Ɔda ho frɛ hɛn dɛ yɛndɔ N'
Dwumadzim' nye ahomgyem',
Ma ɔkyɛn adze nyina.

CAN 45
5 . Jesus frɛ hɛn! O Agyenkwa,
Hɛn 'koma nyɛ setsie mma Wo,
Yɛndɔ W' nkyɛn adze nyina.
Yɛserɛ W', ma yɛntse Wo frɛ n',

CAN 46
1 . Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me,
Dza ɔfa Christ N' enyimnyam ho
Dza ɔfa No dɔ so ho.
Ereka kyerɛ abofra;
Jesus no dɔ ho asɛm.
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me,
Ka 'sɛm no pefee kyerɛ m' dɛ
Minnyi ahom, mo ho fi.
Na meyɛ mberɛw na mafona,
Sunsum ndzɛmbam' asɛm,

CAN 46
2 . Tɔ w' bo ka 'sɛm no kyerɛ me,
Ahanamakye bɔsu
Ɔdze yɛ bɔn edur.
Ewia fir a ɔpa.
Na meetum medze esie-
Na meyar awerɛfir;
Nyame No werdam kɛse a
Si do mber pii ka kyerɛ m'

CAN 46
3 . Ka 'sɛm no bɔkɔɔ kyerɛ me,
Dɛ ema m' akomatɔm'
Jesus bɛpeer mo nkwa,
Ka 'sɛm no mber nyinara,
Kaa dɛ meyɛ bɔnyɛnyi a
Nwinwin mu dɛ ehiasɛm,
Sɛ epɛ ampaara
Wɔ ahokyer ber biaram'.

CAN 46
4 . Ka ' sɛm kor n' ara kyerɛ me,
Aber a isuro dɛ
Christ Jesus bɔ w' esu!
Jesus no dɔ ho asɛm.
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ m' dɛ,
Ka 'sɛm dadaw no kyerɛ me,
No so regye mo do a,
Nyew, na ɔsor n' enyimnyam
Ridzi m' adwen dodow.
Wiadze enyimnyam huhuw n'

CAN 47
1 . Idzii mbuada adaduanan
Adaduanan wɔ sar no do
Adzekyee nye adzesaa,
Wɔsɔɔ Wo hwɛe na annyɛ bɔn.

CAN 47
2 . Ewia sii Wo do adzekyee,
Bɔw tɔɔ Wo do anago,
Edaa fam', isum ɔbo.
Mbowa abɔyafo paar wo ho,

CAN 47
3 . Ma yɛnsɔw Wo bene no bi,
Na yɛnye Wo nweɔn mpaabɔm',
Nye Wo nsɔw yaw ahoɔdzenm'.
Yɛmpow wiadze edzifodze;

CAN 47
4 . Sɛ abɔnsam dze ebufuw
Dom hɛn mma yaannhwe ase.
Toa honam anaa sunsum,
'Wo a edzi no do nyim pɛn,

CAN 47
5 . Nna yebenya W' asomdwee;
Dɛ mbrɛ abɔfo soom Wo n',
Dɛw krɔnkrɔn bɛyɛ hɛndze;
Wɔbɛhyerɛn hɛn so hɛn ho.

CAN 48
1 Fɔdzifo a mayew, 'Wo na 'botum agye me.
Jesus, motwer Wo, medze me kra twer Wo,
Motwer Wo dɔ no na mohwehwɛ W' enyim;
W' adom nwanwa no ntsi na muhuhor Wo.
. Jesus, motwer Wo, medze me kra twer Wo,
Ɔwo wui maa abɔn, Ɔwo wui maa me.
Fɔdzifo a mayew, 'Wo na 'botum agye m',
Obi nnyi sor anaa ase a ɔnye W' sɛ;

CAN 48
2 . Jesus, m' bɔtwer Wo, m' bɔtwer Wo Kyerɛwsɛm;
Ma mentsena W' anan ho ara mintsie.
Osiandɛ matse Wo mbɔbɔrhu ndze no.
Wo Sunsum kyerɛkyerɛ m' a, ɔyɛ m' dɛw dodow,

CAN 48
3 . Jesus, m' bɔtwer Wo, mobɔdwen W' akwan do,
Ewɔ wiadze n' eyɛɛ dɔ nye mbɔbɔrhu,
Hɔn mu biara ho annyɛ Agyenkwa nkɔw.
Ndzebɔnyɛfo fɔɔr Wo, 'kwatafo hwehwɛɛ W',

CAN 48
4 . Jesus, ' bɔtwer Wo, mennkɛgye Wo kyim da,
Obiara a ɔba Wo nkyɛn no emmpam no.
W' anohoba si pi, Wo bɔgyaa som bo;
'Wo nye me kra no nkwagye, me nyankopɔn.

CAN 49
1 . Mma nnsu mma Nyia ɔso mbeamudua
Ɔapen dɛ obowu.
Ɔnnserɛ dasanyi ne nyinsu,
Dze rokɔ Calvary no;

CAN 49
2 . Yaw huhu bi a atow N' enyim,
Mmfir amenhyɛ anaa 'nyimguase:
Oegura ne nyimpadua n',
Onnsuro mbeamudua n'.

CAN 49
3 . Yaw wenwen a ɔbor do yi,
Ahoguan a ɔnnka,
Dza Wo dɔ nnya mu ahotɔ yi,
Wo nko so ne nyina.

CAN 49
4 . Ohu akra a hɔn ntsi oruwu
Dɛ wɔtar hɔn bɔn ho,
Hɔn a ɔsor-man dzi wɔ hɔn
Wɔmmpɛ dɛ wɔhɛn mu.

CAN 49
5 . Ao, ma menye Wo ndzi Wo yaw,
Bepira Wo dɔ akoma,
Dze yaw bɛhyɛ Wo do.   Amen.
Munsu dɛ emi mo bɔn

CAN 5
1 . HOM nkotow Hen nyimnyamfo a ɔwɔ sor;
Ahoɔfɛw nye No buw, ayɛyi abɔ N' do.
Hɛn kyɛm nye hɛn Gyefo, Mbersantsen Panyin,
Mfa ndaase nkamfo No tum nye No dɔ;

CAN 5
2 . Hom ntow No tum nye N'adom so ho ndwom:
N'atar nye ekan, No buw pretetee;
N'ebufuw tseaseanam hye senaman fua tum,
No kwan yɛ sum wɔ ehum atsaban do.

CAN 5
3 . Asaase nye N'anwanwadze a wɔnnka:
Na edze epo abᴐ no ho abᴐmprᴐw.
Nam 'mom a wɔnndan n' da etsim no pintsinn,
Otumfo! Wo tum bɔɔ adze fi tsetse;

CAN 5
4 . W'ayamúyie no gyirama hɛn botúm aká?
Na ɔsɔw fénemfénem wɔ bɔw nye
nyankom mu.
Ofi akoko do pem siansian sar mu,
Ogú ahom wɛ wimú, ɔhyerɛn kan mu;

CAN 5
5 . Huntuma m' mbá a yɛnnkye so yɛyɛ mbérɛw,
Hɛn Bɔfo, hɛn Gyefo, Pomfo na Dɔfo!
Hɛn wérɛ hyɛ Wo mu, W'ayamúyie
Mbrɛ W'adom dua gow a otsim hɔ dú ewiei,
mmpada;

CAN 5
6 Amen.
. Tum a wonnsusu! Dɔ a onnyi kabea!
Abɔdzé adedafamú so nam hɛn mbérɛwyɛ m'
Bɔtonton Wo atow ndwom eyi W' ayaw!
Mbér a abɔfo dzé enyigye tow ndwom no,

CAN 50
1 . Yaw Nyimpa! Wɔnhwɛ dzin bi a
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!
Ɔbɛgyee adasa nkwa
Wɔdze frɛɛ Nyame Ne Ba a

CAN 50
2 . Wɔhyɛɛ N' fɛr, woyii N' ehi,
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!
No bɔgyaa sii m' fakyɛ pi:
Wɔdze m' afɔdzi soaa No;

CAN 50
3 . Yedzi fɔ, hɛn ho yɛ nkɔw
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!
Bo adwe koraa!- aso ampa?
Na Ɔno nye mpata-guan:

CAN 50
4 . Ɔsɛn wimu na owui,
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!
Ɔkaam' dɛ, Afei mewie!
N-dɛ wɔakrɔn No wɔ sor

CAN 50
5 . Na hɛn Enyimnyam Hen n' ɔba
Alleluia! Ɔgyefo bɛn a!
Ber n' yɛbɔtow ndwom yi bio:
Ɔbɛfa No nkorɔfo kɔ a,

CAN 51
1 . Aa! Jesus krɔnkrɔn, ebɛn na ayɛ,
Ao, mandzehunyi.
Atamfo si W' atwetwe, wodze apa W',
Na nyimpa dze enyitan bu Wo fɔ yi?

CAN 51
2 . Woana dzi so? Woana dze yi baa Wo do?
Ao, Jesus, mo bɔn na ɔabɔ W' mbusu yi;
Mara a, Wura Jesus, emi na mepaa W':
'Mi mobɔɔ W' mbeamuduam':

CAN 51
3 . Wodze Guanhwɛfo n' abɔ afɔr ama nguan n';
Akowaa ayɛ bɔn, Ba n' agye ho ntsea;
Ber a nyimpa noara no nkwagye nnyɛ n' asɛm,
Nyankopɔn per no.

CAN 51
4 . 'Mi ntsi, Jesus pa, na ebɛyɛɛ nyimpa,
'Mi mo nkwagye ntsi a.
Wo wum' ahoguan, W' amandzehu yawyaw,
Wo wuyaw wenwen, na wo nkwa afɔrbɔ;

CAN 51
5 . Dɛm ntsi, Jesus pa, dɛ murunntum kaw tua 'i,
Hwɛ W' ayamuhyehye na Wo dɔ a ɔnnsakyer,
Muhuhor Wo, mobɔsɔr ama Wo daa,
Nnyɛ dɛ mefata.

CAN 52
1 . Kokwaa bi wɔ ekyirkyir noho,
Hɔ na wɔsɛɛn Ewuradze a
Kurow bi ban ekyir,
Owui dze gyee hɛn nkwa n'.

CAN 52
2 . Yennkotum yeehu, yɛakyerɛ yaw
A ɔsɔwee no dur;
Ɔsɛɛn hɔ na owui.
Na yɛgye dzi dɛ hɛn ntsi na

CAN 52
3 . Owui ma yeenya bɔnfakyɛ,
Ewiei n' yaakɔ sor manm'.
N' adehye bɔgya n' aagye hɛn,
Owui ma yaayɛ yie,

CAN 52
4 . Obi nnyihɔ a oye dɛ Ɔno
Na ɔdze hɛn kɔ mu.
Na oeetua  bɔn ho kaw n';
No nko na otum bue sor abow n'

CAN 52
5 . O, ɔdɔ bɛn na ɔadɔ hɛn
Otwar dɛ yɛdɔ N' bi,
Yɛper yɛ no ndwuma.
Yɛtwer No bɔgyaa a ɔapon hɛn n',

CAN 53
1 . Nyame Eguambaa, yɛrekaa,
Fi sor noho gye hɛn do,
Kaa hɛn a yɛdwen Wo ho;
Na bohu hɛn mbɔbɔr:
Na gye kra biara a ɔreper;
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!
O, yɛserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Wo dɔ a woepira no n',

CAN 53
2 . W' amandzehu yayaw no,
Bubu hɛn mpokyerɛ mu na
Gye hɛn emumuyɛ nyinam';
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!
O, yeserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Wo bɔgyaa fifir no,
Wo dɔ a ɔmaa iwui ntsi,
Yɛserɛ W' , yi hɛn bɔn kɔ;

CAN 53
3 . Gyedzi mfa Wo bɔgyaa no
Na ma yɛnkɔ asomdweem'!
Nsɔw hɛn bɔfakyɛ ano;
Ntsi, twa hɛn yaw nye fona do;
O, yɛserɛ W', kaa Calvary,
Si n' pi dɛ woebu hɛn bem,
W' amandzehu wɔ dua n' do
Yɛ hɛn yar nyina edur;

CAN 54
1 . Moto m' enyi hwɛ anwanwa dua a
Enyimnyam Hen no tɔɔr do n' a,
M' adze pa biara mummbu n' hwee,
M' ahopɔw nyina yɛ m' nkɔnkɔw.

CAN 54
2 . Mo Wura, ɔmpar me dɛ m' botuw,
Egyangyandze a modɔ kɛse n',
Gyedɛ m' Agyenkwa No wu  mu:
Mobɔ n' afɔr ma No bɔgyaa.

CAN 54
3 . Hwɛ mbrɛ yaw na ɔdɔ rosɔn
Dɛm dɔ na yaw yi mmbɔɔ mu pɛn,
Na nsoɛ kyɛw yi bi nnsoaa bi da.
Ne tsir, Ne nsa, nye N' anan ho:

CAN 54
4 . Wiadze nyina yɛ medze mpo a,
Dɔ nwanwa yi, Nyame dɔ yi,
Gye me kra, mo nkwa, m' adze nyina.
N-kyɛ ɔyɛ akyɛdze a osuar koraa;

CAN 55
1 . Onyame dɔ! 'bɛn na ayɛ 'i?
Bɛkyebo Nyame ewu ama m'!
Egya No domankoma Ba N'
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.
Soaa mo bɔn nyina wɔ dua n' do;

CAN 55
2 . Akwantsemfo nyina hom nhwɛ
Abɔn hom Bɔfo na oruwu 'il!
Aso yaw bi nye Nedze 'i sɛ?
Hom nye m' mbɔsɔ No bɔgyaa nhwɛ:
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.
N-kwa na Asomdwee Hen ruwu!

CAN 55
3 . Woeku No ama wo nye me,
Fakyɛ pem Ne mfem' ma obiara;
Hom ngye Nsɛmpa n' ara ndzi dɛ,
Jesus bɔgyaa pon hɛn nyina,
Ma yɛnye Nyame abɔ mu:
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.

CAN 55
4 . Wɔmma yɛnko dua n' n' ase ha,
Mma yɛnndwen hwee, yɛnnka  hwee, dɛ
Mo Wura, mo Dɔ, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam'.
Yembu adze nyina ahwerdze,
Yɛmfa dɛw ndɔw yarsa nsu n' bi,
Yengyaa hɛn akomam' mma No;

CAN 56
1 . Hom mbra ma yɛnka mmɔm kakra;
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Hom mbra Agyenkwa Ne nkyɛn ha;
Hom mbra ma yɛmbɔm', yɛnka mmɔm:

CAN 56
2 . Worisi No atwetwe yi,
Ana yennkosu ama No?
Ao! hwɛ mbrɛ ɔayɛ komm sɛn hɔ:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.

CAN 56
3 . Wɔbɔɔ Ne nsa nye N' anan mu
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Mbusu dze sum hyɛɛenyi do:
Ne men mu wewee, nsukɔm twaar No!

CAN 56
4 . Ɔkaa ɔdɔ nsɛm mpɛn esuon;
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Ndɔnhwer ebiasa na ɔtaa dzinn
Serɛɛ mbɔbɔrhu maa adasa:

CAN 56
5 . Ma yengyina mbeamudua n' ase,
Ɔbɔhor hɛn ho bɔn nyina:
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Na bɔgya a ofi Ne mfem' no,

CAN 56
6 . Koma bobɔe na nyinsuwa,
Dɔ ahyɛse nye 'koma bobɔe:
Mo Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Wɔmmfa nnkam hɔn a wobisa;

CAN 56
7 . Onyame dɔ! nyimpa no bɔn!
Hɛn Wura Jesus, wɔabɔ N' mbeamuduam.
Munnsu 'i asɔ hom tum ahwɛ;
Na Nyame dɔ edzi konyim:

CAN 57
1 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu!
David ne Ba, wiadze Gyefo.
N-tar saw abowa no do;
Tsena do, na eyɛ Ɔhen mu,

CAN 57
2 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu!
Ɔwo na Sion rotweɔn Wo;
Egu Wo kwan mu dɛ fa do.
Wɔdze n-tar nye mberɛnkɔnson

CAN 57
3 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu!
Ɔkatakyi, hell ne sɛɛfo;
To hɔ petee ma Wo nkorɔfo.
'Wo na ibue sor ahenman

CAN 57
4 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu?
Ana akɔko W' ahengua do.
Dɔmtutuw fi sor rohwɛ Wo,
Dɛ 'rokɔbɔ afɔr huhu

CAN 57
5 . Ko do  kɔ kan ahentum mu!
Dzi nyim, brɛ hɛn 'komatɔmu,
Ndzeyɛtsenenee, ɔdɔ, nye siar.
Wiadze nyina hɛn Enyidar!

CAN 58
1 . Hwɛ adasa hɔn Agyenkwa
Dɔ a ɔkaa N' ma okyii bɔgya
Wɔ enyimguase dua n' ho!
Wui maa wo n' so so pa!

CAN 58
2 . Tsie, ɔrepen! abɔdze rihim,
Abotan repaapaa.
Asaase rowosow;
Asɔrdan mu ntwamutam atsew,

CAN 58
3 . Oewie! wer a ho hia n' ɔatɔ;
Ɔabɔ n' adze ewu!
Ɔrekam', Gye Mo sunsum!
Hwɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ Ne tsir adze,

CAN 58
4 . Na obobu wu apon mu ntsɛm,
Dɔ bɛn nye Wodze sɛ?
Na ɔahyerɛn enyimnyamm';
Nyame Eguambaa, yaw bɛn a,

CAN 59
1 . Yɛtow ayɛyindwom kamfo
Jesus a owuu mbeamudua do n':
N-dzebɔnyɛfo enyidar;
Ne ntsi yemmbu wiadze yi hwee.

CAN 59
2 . Ne mbeamudua no kyerɛ petee
Ɔdze Nyame adom brɛ hɛn.
Ɔsoa hɛn bɔn wɔ dua no do;
Ma yehu dɛ Nyame nye dɔ:

CAN 59
3 . Ne mbeamudua n' yi hɛn afɔdzi;
Ɔhyɛ hɛn dzen mbusu ber mu;
Ɔma dza ɔyɛ wen yɛ dɛw.
Ɔtaa hɔn a wɔtɔ bitsi;

CAN 59
4 . Ɔma ohufo mbanyinndam;
Ɔhyɛ okotoo dzen ma ɔko;
Ɔma kan hyerɛn hɛn wumpa do,
Mma yennsuro samanadze.

CAN 59
5 . O Jesus, Wo mbeamudua no yɛ
Abɔfo kamfo Wo dɔ daa.
Ɔbra ne dɛw, mbusu n' edur
N-dzebɔnyɛfo guandɔbea:

CAN 6
1 . O SƆR Ewuradze wɔ krɔnkrɔnyɛ fɛɛfɛw mu
Fa setsie mapa ɔnye mbrɛhoadze huanhuam,
Kotow huhor No, Ne dzin nye Ewuradze.
Kotow N'enyim, bɔ N'enyimnyam dawur;

CAN 6
2 . Fa w'adwendwen adzesoa to N'ananadze,
Ɔbɔsoa ama wo wɔ N'akoma mu,
Ɔbɛkyekye wo werɛ, na oetsie wo mpaabɔ,
Na oegya w' taataa dɛ.mbrɛ oye ma w'.

CAN 6
3 . Mma nnsuro dɛ ebɛhɛn N'abangua do hɔ,
Afɔrbɔdze a wɔdze gu N'afɔrmbukyia do
Dɛ ahodze a ewɔ no suar ntsi:
Nye nokwar fɛɛfɛw na ɔdɔ mapa.

CAN 6
4 . Yinom, sɛ yɛdze ba suro na ahopopo m' mpo a,
Ɔbɛgye wɔ dzin a ɔsorn bo no ntsi;
Ɔbɛpepa hɛn nyinsu, ɔama yeedzi dɛw,
Oetu hɛn suro, ɔarna hɛn awerɛhyɛm'.

CAN 6
5 . O sɔr Ewuradze wɔ krɔnkrɔnyɛ fɛɛfɛw mu!
Amen.
Fa setsie mapa ɔnye mbrɛhoadze huanhuam,
Kotow huhor No, Ne dzin nye Ewuradze.
Kotow N'enyim, bɔ N'enyimnyam dawur;

CAN 60
1 Mbeamudua n' mu, mbeamudua n' mu,
Na menhyehyɛ moho,
Nkɛpem dɛ me kra bɔhom
Wɔ esutsen n' ekyir hɔ.
. Jesus, fa m' sie mbeamudua n' ho,
Fi Calvary koko no do
Hɔ na nsu a ɔyɛ edur n'
Pem kwa ma obiara.

CAN 60
2 . Mbeamudua n' ho na dɔ na adom
Adzekyee Nworaba hyɛnhyɛnn n'
Ne nserɛmɛn hyerɛɛn mo do.
Too me kra bɔbɔfo;

CAN 60
3 . Dza osii mbeamudua no ho n',
Ao, boa me ma mennantsew
No nwin ase daa daa.
Nyame Eguambaa, yi kyerɛ m';

CAN 60
4 . M' bɔweɔn matweɔn mbeamudua n' ho,
Mahwɛ kan ekodu
Sika man no n' esuegya
Wɔ esutsen n' ekyir hɔ.

CAN 61
1 . Bura bi wɔ hɔ bɔgya ma,
Na ndzebɔnyɛfo bɔtɔm' a,
Wɔtwee n' Immanuel mfem',
Wɔyew hɔn ho fi nyina.

CAN 61
2 . Owifo no ɔdze dɛw hun
Bura n' wɔ n' aber do;
Hɔ na kaansa mo ho yɛ nkɔw a,
M' bɔhor mo ho bɔn nyina.

CAN 61
3 . Nyame Eguambaa, Wo bɔgyaa
Gyedɛ W' asɔrmba nyina enya nkwa,
Mma wɔnnkɛyɛ bɔn bio.
No tum ɔnnkɛpa da,

CAN 61
4 . Ofitsi dɛ me gyedzi hun
Esu a ofi Wo mfem',
Na ɔbɛyɛ edu wum'.
Onyame dɔ ayɛ mo ndwom,

CAN 61
5 . Na owu ma me gyirama
Akamfo Wo wɔ sor.
Me kra bɔtow ndwom dɛɛdɛw bi
Yɛ komm da dɛtsem' a,

CAN 62
1 . O tsir Krɔnkrɔn, wopiraa Wo,
Ɔnam ahoguan ntsi;
Dze sii Wo atwetwe!
Enyim a nkyɛ ɔkyɛn wi,
Hwɛ mbrɛ oesi enyam.
Mbrɛ W' enyim esi atow,
Wɔdze nsoɛ yɛɛ W' ahenkyɛw
Yaw mbordo hyɛɛ Wo do,

CAN 62
2 . Enyimnyam nye nkwa Wura,
Abɔn nya mu mfaso;
Ɔwo na inyaa wuyaw.
Dɛw ka m' dɛ 'yɛ medze.
Dɛw krɔnkrɔn bi a nkyɛ ewɔ a!
Emi mbom na motoo mbra,
Mekenkan nsɛm nwanwa yi a
W' awerɛhow n', W' ayamuhyehye n',

CAN 62
3 . Minya gyirama wɔ hen
Dze eyi Wo ayɛw
Mma memmpa W' ara da;
Mo Wura, fa m' yɛ Wodze koraa;
Pa gu ma m' dɛ m' betsiatsia
W' anwanwa dɔ yi do!
Wɔ W' amandzehu wu yi,
Wo tsema a ɔmmbɔ adze yi?

CAN 62
4 . Muruwu a, mo Wura, bɛn me;
Ao, tu faa bra bohwim me,
Ao, yi Woho kyerɛ m'
Bɛgye m' fi mbusu nsa;
Gyedzi ntom' mma n' enyiwa
Na nyia owu gyedzi mu n'
Ontsim Jesus Wo do;
Wo dɔ ma owu sɔnn.   Amen.

CAN 63
1 . EWURADZE Christ asoɛr ndɛ:
Alleluia!
Ɔsor ntow, wiadze ngye do:
Hom mma dɛw na ehurusi do:
Nyimpa nye abɔfo ka:

CAN 63
2 . Ɔdɔ edzi dwuma no;
Alleluia!
Ɔako, oedzi nyim koraa:
Ɔbo nye aweɔmfo n' yɛɛ kwa;
Christ efi samanadze:

CAN 63
3 . Hɛn enyimnyam Hen tse ase;
Alleluia!
Owu, wo hwirom wɔ hen?
Owu, wo konyim wɔ hen?
Prɛko na owui gyee hɛn:

CAN 63
4 . Wɔakrɔn hɛn Wura Christ wɔ sor;
Alleluia!
Mbeamudua n' nye sor man n' hɛndze a:
Yedzi N'ekyir rokɔ hɔ;
Yɛtse dɛ Ɔno a, yɛbɔsoɛr;

CAN 63
5 . Hɛn enyimnyam Hen siarfo!
Alleluia!
Na yɛkamfo, yɛdɔ Wo.
N-kwa a onnyi ewiei nye dɛ,
Yehu Wo, yɛtse Wo tum,

CAN 64
1 Hallelujah!
. Jesus Christ asoɛr n-dɛ,
Dze poom hɛn a yɛayew no,
Hɛn konyim dapɔn krɔnkrɔn,
Ogyaam wɔ Mbeamudua no do,

CAN 64
2 . Wɔmma yɛmfa ayɛyindwom,
Ɔsɔɔw Mbeamudua nye wumaa,
Dze poon abɔn gyee hɔn nkwa n'.
Ntonton Christ, hɛn sor Hen a,

CAN 64
3 . Na amandze a ohunii n',
Afei odzi hen wɔ sor,
Ɔdze nkwagye abrɛ hɛn;
Mbrɛ abɔfo tow ndwom daa.

CAN 64
4 . Yɛntow ndwom mma hɛn Nyame,
Ɔsormba, hom nyi N' ayɛw,
Egya, Ba, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn.
Nkamfo No dɔ afebɔɔ,

CAN 65
1 Christ asoɛr ewufo mu.
Christ asoɛr o! Hallelujah!
Hɛn konyim adamfo asoɛr.
Wonyi N' ayɛw! Hallelujah!
. Christ asoɛr o! Hallelujah!
Christ asoɛr ewufo mu.
Dɛ Ne kan ahyerɛn bio;
Hɛn 'koma dze ndaase tonton N',
Hɛn konyim adamfo asoɛr.
Wonyi N' ayɛw! Hallelujah!
Yɛdze dɛw bu ntwɛr wɔ N' enyim,
Yɛsoɛr fi yaw na nyinsuam.

CAN 65
2 . Christ asoɛr! No wiadze abrabɔm'
Abɔfo dzi N' ekyir roweɔn N'
Asan aba nkwa mu bio;
Awerɛhow nyina abɔ adze,
Ɔasoɛr, oedzi konyim ndɛ
Ɔnam enyigye mbotsen mu
'Nyimnyam abɔ N' abɔtsir.
Owu na hɛll akotow No;

CAN 65
3 . Christ asoɛr! ofitsi ndɛ dze
Ekyingye na mbɔbɔryɛ nyina
Hom mma yɛnsoɛr yɛnhyɛ fa.
Na suro abɔ adze;
Ndɛ da yi nye No wusoɛr da,
Owu na hɛll remmen hɛn,
Yeedzi adze nyina do nyim;
Yɛyɛ Christ dze, Wɔ No mu na

CAN 66
1 Hallelujah!
. Ewuradze Christ asoɛr bio;
Christ ebubu mpokyerɛ nyinam';
Rotow ndwom wɔ sor daa daa:
Tsie, abɔfo robɔ se,

CAN 66
2 Hallelujah!
. Nyia ɔdze No nkwa maa hɛn n',
Ɔno a hɛn ntsi ɔsɔɔw ko n'
Ɔyɛ hɛn Mpataguan ndɛ;
Hɛn so dɛw tow ndwom dɛ:

CAN 66
3 Hallelujah!
. Nyia ɔsɔɔw obene nyina
Ɔtse enyimnyam' wɔ sor ndɛ,
No werɛ hoow wɔ mbeamudua n' do n',
Odzi ma hɛn, tsie hɛn su.

CAN 66
4 Hallelujah!
. Ɔno a wɔnnto No kwan dzin,
Ɔno a osianee kɔr hɛll,
Ndɛ wɔasoa N' 'henkyɛw wɔ sor.
Nyia katakyi too n' mpokyrɛ n'

CAN 66
5 Hallelujah!
. Ɔno a ɔdaa nda n' mu n'
Dɛ Eguambaa N' yɛ ahemfo Hen.
Ndɛ wohua N' Christianman mu
Wɔakrɔn No dɛ ɔngye nkwa;

CAN 66
6 Hallelujah!
. Ndɛ ɔse yɛmbɔ n' dawur
Mbrɛ abɔn besi enya nkwa,
Mbrɛ hɛn so bɛyɛ ahɛn sor,
Mbrɛ nnuhofo enya fakyɛ

CAN 66
7 Hallelujah!
. Hɛn Mpataguan N' nye W' ampa
Christ, nyɛn Wo nkorɔfo ndɛ;
Ma hɛn nyina atow ndwom dɛ:
Yi hɛn bɔn na hɛn mfom kɔ,

CAN 67
1 Alleluia!
. Ɔko kɛse no abɔ adze;
Afei hɛn Sahen edzi nyim;
Wɔnhyɛ ehurusi ndwom n' ase:

CAN 67
2 Alleluia!
. Owu hyehyɛɛ no dɔm petsee,
Na Christ abɔ hɔn apetse;
Wɔmbɔ se ntow enyigye ndwom:

CAN 67
3 Alleluia!
. Aweɛhow ndaansa no etwam';
Ɔasoɛr konyim mu efi wum';
Enyimnyam nka Hen tseasefo n';

CAN 67
4 Alleluia!
. Ewuradze, W' amandzehu ntsi,
Gye Wo nkowaa fi wu no bɔr mu,
Ma yeenya nkwa, yaatow Wo ndwom:

CAN 68
1 Alleluia!
. Christ tse ase! afei Owu,
Christ tse ase! yi ma yehu
Dɛ samanadze nnkɛmen hɛn.
Wo hu nnkotum etu hɛn bo;

CAN 68
2 Alleluia!
. Christ tse ase! sor nye asaase
Hɛn so yɛbɔkɔ Ne nkyɛn,
Tum nyina wɔdze ama No;
Yɛnye N' ekedzi Hen sor hɔ.

CAN 68
3 Alleluia!
. Christ tse ase! hɛn ntsi owui;
Dɛm ntsi yɛbɛtsena ama No,
Yɛatsew nyɛe nye adwen ho,
Yɛdze hɛn bra eyi N' ayɛw.

CAN 68
4 Alleluia!
. Christ tse ase! yenyim ampa
Dɛ hwee nnkɛpaa hɛn No dɔ ho;
Nnkɔtwe hɛn efi No ho da.
Wu o, n-kwa o, samanadze o,

CAN 68
5 Alleluia!
. Christ tse ase! afei owu
Ber a wu no sum bɔtɔ hɛn.
Yɛ onnyiewiei nkwa abotsen;
Yi bɛka hɛn bo atɔm',

CAN 69
1 . Tsetse mbobow, hom mbuebue
Enyimnyam Hen n' reba o!
fie:
Sahen n' dze ndɔmmum reba
Wonhyira N', wɔmma No mbo.
yie!

CAN 69
2 . Mununkum kumbɔɔ yi ase ε?
Nkɔntwe pii yi so dεn?
Wɔmfa abɔso nhyɛ N'.
Werdam son no oewie pεsɛɛ;

CAN 69
3 . Konyim Damfo kɔ sor no sor,
Ɔse, ɔfata nwionn;
Naaso ɔbεba bio.
No sor-kɔ tɔ N'Asɔr bobor,

CAN 69
4 . Orisiesie adampan pii
N'Egya N'abanyimfa na ofi
Soma Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn.
Wɔ hɛn Egya kurowm';

CAN 69
5 . Ɔrennkyɛr san; hɛn Nkwa bɛba
Abɛfa hɛn ako.
Ɔsor noho mbrɛ wu nndu da
Na hɛn so yεbɔkɔ.

CAN 69
6 . Wiadze Kasamaafo Kortoo
Ama Ne gyedzinyi.
Ɔakrɔn emi saa yi;
Ɔapɛ enyimnyam kokroko

CAN 69
7 . Ɔsor ndomba, mma hom
Ɔba Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn!
Enyimnyam nka Nyame Egya,
nngyaa da,
Nsiesie aka abɔn;

CAN 7
1 . HƐN akoma, nsa nye ndze
Ɔayɛ anwanwadze,
Ɔdze dɔ akyɛ dze
Ehyira hɛen kwan nyina m',
Na ɔda ho yɛ hɛndze.
Ofi hɛn na ne yamu,
Wiadze dzi ho ehurusi;
Yɛdze da nyame ase;

CAN 7
2 . Ɔkyɛso Nyankopɔn
Ɔmfa ahotɔ krɔnn,
Ɔndom hɛn akoma daa,
Ɔnka hɛn ho daa nyina,
Ɔnkora hɛn N'adom mu,
Na ɔmpa hɛn mbusu,
Ongya hɛn nkɔntɔnkye m',
Sesei na ndaamba so.

CAN 7
3 . Ayεyi nye ndaase
Ɔkorsa Nyankopɔn
Ɔnkã Nyame sor Egya,
Ɔtse dɛm afebɔɔ.    Amen.
Mbrɛ ahyɛse ɔtse n'.
Nye Ne Ba Kortonoo,
Nye Nyame Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn:
Sor nye asaase sɔr No;

CAN 70
1 Alleluia!
. Hwɛ da a Christ fowee kɔr sor;
Ɔannkyɛr adasamba nkyɛn,
Ma hɛn enyi egyina N'
Na ɔasan kɔ no sor fie.

CAN 70
2 . Wɔrotweɔn wɔabɔ No se:
Hom nyina mbuebue petee,
Ma Enyimnyam Hen n' nkɔ mu.
M-botsen n' mma hɔn tsir do;

CAN 70
3 . Kaansa ɔahɛn ɔsor mpo a,
Ɔasan kɔ N' ahenguam' mpo a,
Ɔda ho dɔ nyimpamba;
Ɔda ho frɛ hɛn Nedze.

CAN 70
4 . Hwɛ! ɔama Ne nsa do sor,
Hwɛ! No dɔ epiratua n';
N-hyira gu N' Asɔr do.
Tsie! N' anofamfa kasa

CAN 70
5 . Hɛn Wura, sɛ afow kɔ sor,
Afa wim' ekyir noho a,
Ma hɛn so hɛn akoma
Nka Wo do nkɔ Nyame manm'.

CAN 71
1 . Hwɛ Konyimdzifo n' afow sor,
Dze Ne tseaseanam fua do
Hallelujah enyigyem',
Hwɛ Hen n' ahyɛ N' ahentar
Na sor mbotsen no ebuebue
Regye hɔn sor Hen akɔm'.
Rokɔ No sor ahemfie;
Tsie! sor adwontow kuw ruhur

CAN 71
2 . Woana na ɔreba 'nyimnyam mu
Ɔaka bɔn na Satan egu,
Ɔko Wura, dɔm Nyankopɔn.
Ɔno a ɔsɔɔw mbeamudua do fona
Ɔno a ofi ndam' soɛree,
Ɔno na oedzi konyim
Ma ehurusi mbɛn ka do 'i?
Nam wu do asɛɛ N' atamfo.

CAN 71
3 . Ɔama hɛn nyimpasu no do
Ɔsor hɔ na yɛbɛtsena,
Ewuradze Tumfo, Wo sorkɔm'
Fi fuam' kɔ Nyame nyimfa;
Jesus dzi hen, abɔfo sɔr N';
Nyame Nyimpa tse ahenguam'
Yɛdze gyedzi hu hɛndze.
Yɛnye N' egyina 'nyimnyam mu:

CAN 71
4 . Enyimnyam nka Egya Nyame;
Ɔno a oenya sor ahenman n'
Enyimnyam a onnyi ewiei nka
Enyimnyam nka Nyame Ba a,
Enyimnyam nka Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn;
Hɔn wɔ sor nye asaase.
Nye Nyame Baasa Kor no
Oewu, ɔasoɛr na ɔafow sor,

CAN 72
1 . Sika mbotsen no ebuebue,
Ɔkɔ N' Egya Ne nkyɛn.
Enyimnyam Hen no ahɛn mu,
Kwan ada mu petee;

CAN 72
2 . Ewuradze, edzi hɛn kan,
Ama yeekefir mbrɛ ewɔ,
Na yeehu Nyame enyim.
'Rekɛpɛ hɛn tsenabew,

CAN 72
3 . Dɛm n-tsi enyimnyam hyerɛn
Fua a osiiw W' hɛn enyi do n',
Hɛn kwan do wɔ asaase;
Kan fi sor hotse no.

CAN 72
4 . Ma hɛn 'koma nye adwen do,
Fa W' adom pa n' dom hɛn,
Hɛn 'koradze ada sor.
Na yɛnenam asaase ha 'i,

CAN 72
5 . Na hɛn enyidar na dɔ eegyina
Nyame nyimfa mbrɛ 'tse n'.
Tsena hɛn mu na ndaamba hɛn so
Yaatsena Wom' afebɔɔ.   Amen.

CAN 73
1 . Mbowa a Jewfo dze bɔɔ afɔr,
Anaa ɔatsew hɛn ho.
Hɔn bɔgyaa nyinara
Nn-kotum ama etsidaa,

CAN 73
2 . Christ, sor Eguambaa n' dze,
Afɔrbɔdze a ɔwɔ dzin,
Na ɔsom bo kyɛn hɔn nyina.
Oyi hɛn bɔn nyina;

CAN 73
3 . Me gyedzi nsa bɛda
Ber a medze nnuho gyina ha
Mereka mo bɔn yi.
W' etsifi pampam' hɔ,

CAN 73
4 . Me kra twa n' enyi hwɛ
Dza obuu Wo kɔn a,
Ma 'sɛn mbusu dua n' do.
Ohu dɛ n' afɔdzi ka ho

CAN 73
5 . Yɛgye dzi a yɛtse dɛ
Mbusu no efi hɔ;
Yɛdze dɛw hyira Eguambaa n',
Yɛtwer N' anwanwa dɔ n'.

CAN 74
1 . Me gyedzi tsim Wo do,
CalvaryEguambaa,
Gyefo Krɔnkrɔn:
Ma ofir ndɛ menyɛ
Morosɔr yi, tsie me;
Wodze koraa.
Yi mo bɔn nyinara;

CAN 74
2 . Ma W' adom kɛse no
Ao, ma mo so mo dɔ
Ɔmfram dzendzen mma Wo
Dɛ mbrɛ iwui maa me n',
Ma menyɛ ndam;
Na mma ɔnndan da.
N-hyɛ m' akoma dzen,

CAN 74
3 . Menam bra sum mu yi,
Ma sum ndan adzekyee,
Mimmfi Wo nkyɛn.
Na yaw etwa mo ho 'i,
Pepa me nyinsuwaEso mma monntɔ gon
Woara kyerɛ m' kwan;

CAN 74
4 . Ber a bra bɔbɔ adze,
Ao, m' Agyenkwa siarfo,
Bɛpram mo do n',
Fa me kra a apon no n'
Kɔ sor fie sɔnn.   Amen.
Na owu n' esutsen
Pa m' suro na ekyingye,

CAN 75
1 Dzi dɛw, mese wo dɛ, Dzi dɛw.
Ma w' akoma nye wo ndze do;
. Dzi dɛw, Nyame yɛ Hen!
Ɔdasanyi, tow ndwom,
Kotow w' Ewuradze;
Na dzi dɛw daa nyina:

CAN 75
2 . Agyenkwa Christ dzi hen,
Ɔgyee egua wɔ sor:
Ɔhoor hɛn ho fi no,
Nokwar nye dɔ dzi wɔ n';

CAN 75
3 . N' ahendzi mmbɔ adze da,
No tum wɔ sor na ase;
Saafee ama Jesus:
Wɔdze samandze;

CAN 75
4 . Ɔtse Nyame nyimfa
Bɔbɔ hɔn mu adze
Edzi N' ahyɛdze do:
Kɛpem dɛ N' atamfo

CAN 75
5 . Obedzi nyim ewie,
Eenya sor enyigye:
Ma dasanyi biara
Oetu hɛn bɔn nyina,

CAN 75
6 . Dzi dɛw enyidadom';
Abɛfa hɛn akɔ
Hɛn domankoma fie:
Hɛn Jesus bɛba bio

CAN 76
1 . O bra, O bra Immanuel,
Bɛba wo nkyɛn, O Israel.
Ɔka mmɔn ananabea ha
Dzi dɛw! Dzi dɛw! Immanuel
Kodu dɛ Nyame Ba bɛba.
Na bɔpɔn ndɔmmum Israel,

CAN 76
2 . O bra, O bra, Wura Tumfo,
Ɔwo a tsetse n' edze mbra
Maa mbusuakuw wɔ Sinai do
Wɔ fua, hu, nye ahentum mu.

CAN 76
3 . O bra jesse Poma, bɛgye
Gye Wo nkorɔfo fi hɛll bun mu,
Ma hɔn konyimdzi wɔ wu do.
Wo man fi Satan tum ase;

CAN 76
4 . O bra, Adzekyee Woraba
Bɔ owu sunsuma petse.
Bɔbɔ anago sum hwetse,
Ma wo mbae nkyenyan hɛn sunsum;

CAN 76
5 . O bra, David Saafee, O bra,
Bue hɛn sor fie pataa ma hɛn,
Na siw dza ɔdze mbusu ba n'.
Yɛ kwan a wɔdze kɔ sor n' sɔnn,

CAN 77
1 . Hwɛ! Ɔdze mununkum risian,
Ahotsewfo mpempem ka ho,
Alleluia!
Dzi N' ekyir kumbɔɔ reba:
Nyame reba ebedzi hen.
Nyia da bi ɔtɔɔr hɛn ntsi n';

CAN 77
2 . Enyienyi nyina bohu No
Da a wobohu Messiah n'.
Dɛ oewuna ahentar wusuww;
Hɔn a woemmbu N' bi, wɔtɔɔn No n',
Wobotwa ewuo,
Wopirapiraa N', bɔɔ N' mbeamudua mu n'

CAN 77
3 . N' amandzehu ho nsɛnkyerɛdze
Bɔhwɛ enyimnyam etua n'.
Da ho ara wowɔ No ho;
Dza N' asomfo a wɔapon hɔn no
Dzi ho ehurusi daa n';
Yɛdze dɛw bɛn

CAN 77
4 . Ɔnyɛ hɔ! nkorɔfo nyina mbu W' ntwɛr
Alleluia!
Gye ahendzi n' yɛ Wodze;
Gyefo, gye tum na enyimnyam no,
Onnyiewiei Nyankopɔn, sian!
Wo domankoma ahengua n' enyim;

CAN 78
1 . Kwantunyi ankonam ne kan,
Adzekyee Woraba,
Fa pam hɛn yaw nyina.
Pue, na tow W' anapa nserɛmɛn n'

CAN 78
2 . Ewuradze siarfo, ma mbeambea
Na nsupruw nyina ntow
Ndwom nyi W' adehye Dzin ayɛw,
Wɔmfa Wo nyɛ hɔn Hen.

CAN 78
3 . Ma wiadze nyinara a afei
Wɔasɛ sor man hyɛnhyɛnn n',
Wɔmfa nkaa Wo dɔ no.
Wɔmma ehurusi ndwom do

CAN 78
4 . Jesus, W' abɔdze risi nkrum-
Asaase, Po, nye wim'-
Kekam' dzendzen frɛ Wo.
Wɔnye hɛn akoma yɛ kor

CAN 78
5 . Mbeamudua n' n' adom, n' asomdwee
Afei enyimnyam ahenkyɛw n'
Na konyim n' nyɛ Wodze.    Amen.
Ne nyinara Wodze a,

CAN 79
1 . BEEBIARA mbrɛ ewia ɔhyerɛn,
Gyedɛ ewia fir dɛ ɔnntɔ bio.
Jesus twa dɛ obedzi hen;
N' ahendzi tsen fi pomu' du pomu',

CAN 79
2 . Asɔr nyina wɔbɛyɛ ama N',
Na wɔdze ayɛyi ebu N' kyɛw;
Ne dzin, tse dɛ eduhuam a,
Nye afɔr nyina botu akɔ sor.

CAN 79
3 . Nkorɔfo na ngyirama mpem nyina
Dze No dɔ ho ndwom dɛɛdɛw mu;
Na mbofra so ma hɔn ndze do,
Wɔtow Hosanna ma Ne dzin.

CAN 79
4 . Mbrɛ odzi hen n', nhyira ahyɛ ma,
Afonafo nya daa ahomka;
Na ehiafo so, wohyira hɔn.
Wotu adaduafo apo;

CAN 79
5 . Beebiara mbrɛ ɔkyerɛ No tum,
Ne mbanana nya ma ɔbor do.
No mu na nhyira a Adam yeew no n',
Wu na mbusu fi hɔ koraa:

CAN 79
6 . Wɔmma abɔdze nyina nsoɛr
M-fa ayɛyɛdze mbrɛ hɔn Hen;
Na asaasemba so nsuo mu ntow.    Amen.
Sor abɔfo mfa ndwom nsian bio,

CAN 8
1 . Me kra, yi ɔsor hen ayɛw,
Ɔapon wo, dze wo bɔn akyɛ w',
Fa w' ayɛdze bra N' enyim;
Woana mbɔ nyi No ayɛw?
Yi bɛkyebo Hen ayɛw.
Yi No ayɛw!

CAN 8
2 . Yi N' ayɛw, Nadom na enyimpa
Ɔka enyim nyaa, ohyira ntsɛm:
Hwɛɛ egyanom ahohiam';
Nyimnyamfo wɔ nokwardzim'.
Yi No ayɛw!
Yi No ayɛw, ɔnnsakyer da,

CAN 8
3 . Ɔhwɛ hɛn, dze fir hɛn dɛ egya;
Ɔgye hɛn atamfo nyina nsam',
Ɔma hɛn do dɔ mu ara,
Dɛ mbrɛ N' adom pem mber nyina.
Onyim hɛn mberɛwyɛ dodow;
Yi No ayɛw!

CAN 8
4 . Sor abɔfo hom nhuhor No;
Ewia, bosoom, hom nkotow, No,
Hom hu N' enyim na enyim;
Hom nye hɛn nyi Nyame ayɛw.    Amen.
Hom nyi N' ayɛw!
Mber na mbea nyinam' abɔdze,

CAN 80
1 . O Nyame Dɔ, sian famu,
Bopue m' akoma mu,
Bra bɔhwehwɛ me kra,
Fa Woara Wo hyew dzendzen bi n' bɔsoɛ mu;
Kyigyinafo e, twe bɛn!
Na ma Wo gya krɔnkrɔn no mbɛfram me kra.

CAN 80
2 . Ma ɔndzɛw ara yie,
Ɔnhyerɛn m' enyim daa,
Ɔnhyerɛn mo ho nye mo kwan mu nyina.
Na ma W' enyimnyam kan n'
Nkodu dɛ ɔbɛhyew
Wiadze akɔndɔ nyina ma ɔaatɔ nso;

CAN 80
3 . Na ma ɔdɔ krɔnkrɔn
Ahobrɛadze 'koma a,
Ɔdze noho to famu,
Ɔnyɛ m' egudo atar,
Na ɔdze nyinsuwa kyir noara n' esintɔ.
Na ma menhyɛ ahobrɛadze wɔ ase;

CAN 80
4 . Dɛm yi na ɔbɛma
Akɔndɔ dzendzen a
Gyedɛ Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn ayɛ n' ne tsenabea.
Mbrɛ n' ahoɔfɛw bɛyɛ n'
Me kra benya no nnkenya kabea mpo;
Obi runntum nnkyerɛ

CAN 81
1 . TSETSEBER a Nyame siaan wiadze n',
Ɔbaa n' tum nye ebufuwm';
Fa yɛɛ sum, fa daan gya.
Fua bɔɔ apetse N' ananadze,

CAN 81
2 . Na ne mprɛnu no a ɔbae no,
Bɔkɔɔ kyɛn anapa mframa
Ɔbaa n' tum nye dɔ mu;
Nna Ebubur Krɔnkrɔn n' bae.

CAN 81
3 . Ogya a osiaan Sinai do no
Ɔdaan enyimnyam ahenkyɛw
Ɔframee ma ɔyɛɛ hu,
Wɔ ahotseweefo tsir do.

CAN 81
4 . Na dε mbrε Israel dze hu
Abεn a abᴐfo mpo suro,
Gyigyee fua kebii mu.
Tsee ndze kεse mbordo n’,

CAN 81
5 . Dεm na hεn Nyame no Sunsum
Bodwiir no nguankuw do n’,
Dε mframa a ᴐyε dzen.
Wᴐtsee ndze fi sor wᴐ mbea nyina,

CAN 81
6 . Ͻhyε Nyankopᴐn N’Asᴐr ma,
Gyedε ntsintsiman ‘koma nko
Nna onnya no mu kwan.
Twa bᴐn wiadze yi ho hyia:

CAN 81
7 . Ewuradze, bra, Nyansa, Dᴐ, Tum,
Bue hέn aso ma yεntse;
Dᴐ mu o, suro mu o, gye hεn. 	Amen.
Mma ᴐgyeber yi mmpa hεn ho,

CAN 82
1 . Egya, hyɛ Wo Ba enyimnyam,
Fa Werɛkyekyefo n' ma hɛn
Jesus dzin ntsi, fa N' ma hɛn.

Yɛ dza Ne mpaabɔ bisa n'':
Yɛnam gyedzi do regye N',

CAN 82

Bɛtsena hɛn akoma mu:
Ɔdze N' adom nye No dɔ
Hɛn mboa nye papa nyina
Na yɛatse Sunsum no nka;
Pem fi No nkotoo mu ba.

CAN 82

CAN 83
1 . Ansaana hɛn Gyefo siarfo
Ɔnye hɛn ntsena.
Nye hɛn ridzi mpaamu n',
Ogyaa hɛn Ɔkwankyerɛfo dɛ

CAN 83

Dɛ ɔatrɛ n' atsabanm',
No nkorɔfo do.

CAN 83

Ɔrebɛkyerɛkyerɛ hɛn;

CAN 83

Na ɔdae ahom dɛɛdɛw bi

CAN 83

Dɛ ewimbir mframa n';

CAN 83

CAN 83

Ɔmfata Wo.    Amen.

CAN 84
1 . Ao o, Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, bra!

Tow Wo kan hyerɔn hɔn do.

CAN 84

Amen

Na fa hɛn kɔ Wo dɛw mu.

CAN 84

CAN 84

CAN 84

Ahohyehyem' ahotɔ,

CAN 84

Hyɛ agyedzifo mu ma.

CAN 85

CAN 85

CAN 85

CAN 85

CAN 86

CAN 87

CAN 88

CAN 88

Nya ahonya mbordo;
Otsim hɔ afebɔɔ.

CAN 88

CAN 88

CAN 88

Na munhu m'Agyenkwa.    Amen.

CAN 89
1 . Sunsum Krɔnkrɔn, bra hɛn 'komam',
Ma yɛntse Wo tum no,
Na kan na dɔ fir Wo.
Wo na tsetse wɔdze W' hyɛɛ nkɔm,

CAN 89

CAN 89
3 . Sor Ebubur, trɛ W' atsabanm'
Butuw hɛn kra no sum no do,
Na ma hɔ ɔnyɛ kann.
Wɔ hɛn isum no do,

CAN 89
4 . Sɛ 'hyerɛn hɛn mu a, yɛnam Nyame
Na yɛnye Wo mba nyina esusu
Nankasa do bohu N',
Onyame dɔ no bun.   Amen.

CAN 9
1 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Wonyi Nyame Hen ayɛw!
Wɔmfa ayɛyindwom mbrɛ N';

CAN 9
2 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Wonyi N' ayɛw: ɔayὲ ewia,
Dὲ ɔkɔ aprɔw daa daa nyina:

CAN 9
3 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Na eso ɔayɛ bosoom,
Ma odu anafua a ɔhyerɛn:

CAN 9
4 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Wonhyira N' dὲ ɔtɔ nyankom,
Ma ɔma edziban fifir:

CAN 9
5 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Na ɔma asaase pa so
Oyi no ndɔbaa ma hɛn:

CAN 9
6 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Ɔama buber so aba,
Ɔahyɛ hɛn asan mama:

CAN 9
7 N' ehumbɔbor tsim hɔ daa,
Osi pi yɛ nokwar daa.
. Ɔama edziban a ɔsen dɛm,
Daa daa dɛw ho ahobadze:

CAN 9
8 Enyimnyam nka Egya, nye Ba,
Nye Sunsum, Ebiasa Kor.   Amen.
. Enyimnyam nka, Hen dɔyɛfo
Abɔdze nyina ntow enyimnyam,

CAN 90
1 . Ewuradze, W' asɛm tsim,
'No na yɛhwɛ nantsew,
Nya kan nye enyigye.
Nyia ɔgye no nokwar

CAN 90
2 . Atamfo ba hɛn do a,
Awerɛkyekyer nsɛmpa,
N-kwagye amandzɛɛ.
W' asɛm yi hyɛ hɛn dzen,

CAN 90
3 . Ɔbra n' ehum tu hɛn,
Na ɔkyerɛ hɛn kwan.
Na sum gye hɛn do a,
Ne kan hyerɛn ma hɛn,

CAN 90
4 . Woana botum akyerɛ
Ahotɔ nye dɛw a
N-tsetsekwaa nyinaa?
W' asɛmpa yi dze ma

CAN 90
5 . Ehumbɔbɔr nsɛmpa,
Ɔboa atseasefo;
Hɔn a wɔda wuso werɛ.
N-kwasɛm, ɔkyekye

CAN 90
6 . Ewuradze, ma yenhu
Daa nyinaa yaabɛn Wo!   Amen.
Na yaadɔ, yeesuro Wo,
No mu adzesua krɔnkrɔn n',

CAN 91
1 . KANEÀ a yɛdze hwɛ hɛn kwan mu,
Adom n-sù a ofi sor tɔ
Ma akwantufo nom bi;
Mma yaammfom kwan yɛannyew;

CAN 91
2 . Edziban a ofi sor tɔ
Ma yɛdze nyɛn hɛn kra:
Mbrɛ ɔsor man mu tse;
Nwomà a yɛkenkan a yehu

CAN 91
3 . ꓛyɛ gyafadum anago,
ꓛbra po tu ne tsir gu do a,
Hɛn sekyɛ nye tabon.
Munumkum adzekyee;

CAN 91
4 . Onyame Twerammpon N' Asɛm,
N' enyimmyam Ba N' Ahyɛmù,
Yeennya wo a yenntum bra yi bɔ,
Yenntum nnya Nyame man.

CAN 91
5 . Ewùradze, dom hɛn ma yensũa
Na yɛmfa mbofra 'koma ngye
Ne nkyѐrɛkyѐrɛ krɔnkrɔn no.
W' Asɛm mu nyansa n' yie,

CAN 92
1 . Ma yɛntow anwanwa dɔ bi ho ndwom,
Anwanwa dɔ
Ɔdɔ a ofi Sor Egya N' akomam'
Ɔwɔ hɛn Ɔsor Egya N' akomam'.
Nokwar ɔdɔ a,
Rehyɛ adasamba ma:

CAN 92
2 . Jesus, Agyenkwa n', dze dɛw sianee bae
Bɛkaa 'Sɛmpa n';
Ɔduaa N' amandzehu pii do hwehwɛɛ
Hɔn a hɔn enyidar asa n'.
Hɔn a wɔayew n',
Otuaa kaw mbordo na ɔgyee hɔn nkwa.

CAN 92
3 . Jesus da ho hwehwɛ hɔn a wɔayew n':
Afonafo, hom mbra fie!
Anwanwa dɔ
Ɔwɔ hɛn Ɔsor Egya N' akomam'.
No dɔ pɛ dɛ ɔkata hɔn bɔn do:
Wokyin yɛ dɛn?

CAN 92
4 . Anwanwa dɔ, bra mo so m'akomam',
Ahobrɛadzem'
Bra bɛtsena hɔ:
Enyiber nye atorsɛm mu.
Na mepɛ dɛ mepɛ Wo suanyi bi.
Tsew me kra ho na oeefi dza ɔnntsenm'-

CAN 93
1 . Ana ahaw, na aberɛ,
Ahomgye.
Na wo kɔn ebu?
Tsie! Obi dɛ, Bra, na m' bɛma w'

CAN 93
2 . Ana akam bi wɔ No a,
Medze m' bohu No?
N' anan ho, Ne nsam', nye Ne mfem'
Wɔ epiratua.

CAN 93
3 . Ana kyɛw bi so N' a ɔma
Ɔyɛ dɛ ɔhen?
Na nsoɛ dze a.
Nyew, ahenkyɛw ara ampa;

CAN 93
4 . Sɛ muhu N' n a meka No do a,
Amandzehu, nye ɔfona,
Ebɛn na m' benya?
Nye nyinsuwa.

CAN 93
5 . Sɛ menngyaa dɛ meka No do a,
'Bɛn na nkyii m' benya?
Botwa mu.
Ɔfona, nye yaw, nye Jordan

CAN 93
6 . Ana mese N' dɛ ɔngye m' a,
Ɔbɛse m', Oho?
Dabi; gyedɛ sor nye asaase
Etwam' kɔ.

CAN 93
7 . Muhu N', ka No do, meper a,
Ahotsewfo nye asɛnkafo
Bua dɛ, Nyew!
Obehyira  m' ampa?

CAN 94
1 'Mi dɛm yi.
. Ewuradze, matse nka dɛ
Edze rofɔw daadze a oetwie,
Ma bi nsosɔ mo so do,
'Rowora nhyira nsu pii,

CAN 94
2 . Mma mmpa mo ho, dɔyɛfo Egya,
Ɔfata dɛ igya m' hɔ dze,
M' akomam' wɔ bɔn so ampa;
Na fa mbɔbɔr hu me so,

CAN 94
3 . Mma mmpa mo ho, Agyenkwa brɛfo,
Ber a 'refrɛ yi frɛ me so,
Ma mondɔ Wo na mentar Wo;
Mo kɔn adɔ W' enyimtsewee;

CAN 94
4 . Mma mmpa mo ho, Sunsum tumfo,
Jesus Ne yie ho Dasefo,
Ka tum kasa n' kyerɛ me so,
'Wo na ibue furafo enyi;

CAN 94
5 . Nyame dɔ krɔnn a ɔnnsaker,
Dua mo so do yi kyerɛ,
Jesus bɔgyaa a ɔsom bo,
Nyame adom a ɔmmbɔ adze n',

CAN 95
1 (Amandzɛɛ n', kyerɛ mu yie)
(Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo)
(Si do ara tow, Si do ara tow)
. Jesus gye ndzebɔnyɛfo;
Amandzɛɛ n' ma wɔntse ase;
Bɔ adomsɛm yim' kyerɛ
Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo
Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo.
Hɔn a wofi sor kwan mu,
Si do tow, si do tow bio;
Wɔahwe ase, reyɛ ekyim.

CAN 95
2 . Bra, ɔbɛma W' ahomgye;
Ɔgye abɔn mu abɔn;
Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo.
Twer No: N' asɛm si no pi:

CAN 95
3 . M' akoma mmubu me fɔ bio,
Apata mbra no koraa.
Mo ho san wɔ mbra n' enyim;
Nyia ɔhoor mo ho fi no

CAN 95
4 . Christ ɔgye ndzebɔnyɛfo,
Ɔnye m' bɛhɛn sor man mu.
Emi mpo a mo bɔn dɔɔ so;
Me nkekae nyinaa botu;

CAN 96
1 . Abɔn, 'kɔbesaefo, hom mbra,
Bahatɔfo, epirafo,
Ɔpɛ, mma hom nngye kyim bio.
Ɔyɛ Tumfo
Jesus rotweɔn agye hom nkwa;
Tsema na tum ahyɛ N' ma;

CAN 96
2 . Hom mbra, akɔhweaban, hom mbra;
Adom a ɔtwe hɛn bɛn N',
Bra Jesus hɔ bɔtɔ bi.
Hom nhuhor Nyame ayamuyie,
Nokwar gyedzi, nnuho mapa,
Wɔmmfa sika,

CAN 96
3 . Hom mbra, hom a hom kɔn ebu,
Abɔn na Jesus bɛfrɛe.
Hom a asehwe epira hom;
Hom nnkɛba dabiarada;
Nnyɛ atsenenee a,
Sɛ hom rotweɔn ayɛ yie ana a,

CAN 96
4 'Yi ɔdze ma w';
. Mma tsibowaba nnyɛ w' mma nkyinkyin,
Ɔyɛ Sunsum 'napawi.
Emudzi a ɔregye ara nye,
Ibohu wo hia a ihia N':
Mma emudzi nnyɛ w' adwendwen,

CAN 96
5 Jesus nkotoo
. Nhwɛ! Nyame-nyimpa N' afow sor,
Fa woho ma N', fa ma N' koraa;
Gyina No bɔgyaa do dzi ma W',
Mma adwen fofor nntwa ntamu!
na otum yɛ abɔn yie.

CAN 97
1 . Bra ma hɛn a yɛgye Christ dzi
N' adom enyimnyam no.
Ntonton hɛn Agyenkwa,
Yɛmfa enyigye ndze nkamfo

CAN 97
2 . Ogyina bɔnyɛnyi biara
Anaa ɔyɛ ma ɔkɔ.
N' akoma ekyir robɔm';
Nyia ɔasɛɛ koraa nnyi dɛ ɔpam N' bio,

CAN 97
3 . Yɛnam adom do tsie Wo ndze,
Dɛ Ɔwo 'bɛhɛn mu.
Pen do dɛ yi hɛn bɔnm',
Yesi pi dzi dɛw enyidarm',

CAN 97
4 . Bra mu ntsɛmara, sor Hɔho,
Na mma mmfi ha nnkɔ da
Nyɛ ɔdomankoma dɔ.    Amen.
Nye hɛn ndzidzi, ma edziban no

CAN 98
1 Agyenkwa, Agyenkwa,
Mma mmpa mo nko ho.
Na 'refrɛfrɛ m' asɛfo yi,
Tsie mo mbɔbɔr su!
. Mma mmpa mo ho, Agyenkwa brɛfo,
Mma mmpa mo nko ho.
'Reyaa W' ano kyerɛ binom,
Tsie mo mbɔbɔr su;

CAN 98
2 . Mbɔbɔr ahengua enyim ha
ma m' akomatɔm';
Mokosɔw ha awerɛhow mu
Na pa m' ekyingye.

CAN 98
3 . Motwer Wo yie no nkotonoo,
Mohwehwɛ W' enyim;
Nam W' adom do gye m'.
Yɛ mo sunsum pirafo edur,

CAN 98
4 . M' aweɛkyekyer n- sunyiwa,
Anaa sor dɛ 'Wo?
Mowɔ woana wɔ ase ha,
'Wo 'kyɛn me nkwa mpo;

CAN 99
1 Jesus yɛ mbɔbɔrhu, ɔbɛgye nkwa.
Per gye hɔn a wɔreyew,
Tse ma hɔn a woruwu,
. Per gye hɔn a wɔreyew,
Hwim hɔn fi bɔn na adakamaa mu:
Ma asehwefo do,
Se hɔn dɛ Jesus tum dɛ ɔgye nkwa.
Su ma dza ɔafom kwan,
Tse ma hɔn a woruwu,

CAN 99
2 . Sɛ wɔmmfa N' nnyɛ hwee mpo a,
Ɔda ho rotweɔn.
Enye hɔn nka n' berɛww;
Enye hɔn nka n' ka pa,
'Rotweɔn ɔba a oenu noho n' ɔagye n'.
Sɛ wɔgye dzi ara a ɔdze bɛkyɛ.

CAN 99
3 . Sɛ abɔnsam daadaa
Dza nkyɛ ɔnntse no afei ɔbɛtse.
Ekyerɛ no Wo dɔ a,
Eyɛ no ayamuyie,
Nyame N' adom twe n' ekyir a ɔyɛ:
'Nyimpa n' akoma a,

CAN 99
4 . Per gye hɔn a wɔreyew:
Dwuma 'i da wo do;
Ewuradze bɛma w' ho ahoɔdzen.
Fa abotar twe hɔn;
Frɛ hɔn ma wɔnsan mbra,
Se kobɔfo n' dɛ Gyefo n' wui maa no.
